- **Sleep**: poor. Workshop activity logs and tower-corridor camera traces indicate a habitual 2–5 a.m. wake window. Carceral residue plus complex grief plus, presumably, the lingering Particle-exposure circadian disruption documented broadly in chronic Pym-tech users.

He turns down two offers to lead a Strike-team subset during this period. The refusals are framed as humility; they are also accurate self-assessment. He should not be leading. He knows it.

---

## 4.3 — Reconciliation Window with Cassie (2019–2021)

The Young Avengers / Children's Crusade-era Cassie was killed; the Cassie of the present canon is the restored version (mechanism: the 2021 *Avengers: The Children's Crusade* completion-arc echoes and the *X-Men/Avengers* reality reconciliations of the late 2010s), who returns to the active continuity as Stinger / later Stature again. Father and daughter are simultaneously alive for the first time in roughly a publication decade.

The reconciliation is not a single event but a graduated thaw across approximately eighteen in-universe months, traceable through panel-marginal evidence:

- **First contact**: a coffee in Brooklyn, neutral ground, Cassie's choice. Lang arrived eleven minutes early, sat outside, did not order until she did. He had rehearsed.
- **Second contact**: a workshop visit, Cassie consulting him on a Pym-Particle harness calibration question. *She approached him as a technical peer.* This is the moment, by panel composition, that the subject's posture changes in the canon. He does not know what to do with being treated as competent by his own daughter. He overexplains. She laughs at him. The laugh is forgiving. He files it carefully.
- **Sustained contact**: by the time of the *Ant-Man* 60th-anniversary mini (Ewing, 2022), Cassie is appearing as a co-protagonist. The dynamic on the page is *cautious-warm*. Neither raises the Power Broker years. Both behave as if a statute of limitations on the betrayal has been mutually, silently agreed.

The non-discussion is itself the relationship's present architecture: a stable bond predicated on a shared agreement not to interrogate the rupture. The file's standing assessment is that this stability is *real but fragile* — the kind of reconciliation that holds until a single new pressure (financial crisis, custodial threat, a request for a favor that flirts with the old patterns) re-opens it. The subject knows this. Cassie likely also knows this. They are both managing it.

Notable behavioral acquisition during this period: the subject begins, for the first time in the documented record, to keep a single photograph of Cassie visible in his quarters. Wallet-sized, taped inside the door of his workshop locker. Not on a desk, not framed — *taped to the inside of a door that closes.* The semantic content of that placement is total. He wants to see her every day. He cannot bear to display her where others might comment.

---

## 4.4 — The Ewing Mini and the Macro-Time Crisis (2022)

Al Ewing's *Ant-Man* (2022) is, formally, a four-issue legacy celebration spanning Pym, Lang, Cassie, and a future Ant-Person. Substantively, for this subject, it functions as a *life review* — the kind of integrative narrative episode that in clinical terms one would expect of a man approaching late midlife.

The subject's segment shows him operating Ant-Man Security Solutions again, this time *solvent*, *legal*, and *small.* He has reduced his ambitions. He works residential and small-commercial gigs. He does not subcontract. He turns down a lucrative offer from a former Power Broker associate within the first issue and does so without visible struggle — the surveillance-significant detail is that he turns it down *before* doing the rationalization-math, not after. This is new. The cognitive narrowing under financial pressure has, in this period, partially released its grip. Inference: the absence of acute Cassie-crisis has allowed the master rationalization to lie dormant long enough that the subject can, for the first time, observe its activation rather than be steered by it.

During the macro-time confrontation in the mini's climax, the subject is briefly de-aged, briefly aged, briefly confronted with the future Ant-Person who carries his legacy. His reaction to the future hero is — *file this* — *not* pride. It is *embarrassment.* He believes the legacy is more than he warrants. The Ewing text is explicit about this on the page. The negative core schema is intact. Cassie, present, observes the embarrassment and names it. He deflects with humor. The 0.7-second latency holds.

---

## 4.5 — The Kang Dynasty Period and Post-Krakoa Adjacency (2023–2024)

The subject's involvement in the *Timeless / Kang* arcs (background ensemble role, MacKay-era *Avengers*) is operational and unobtrusive. He is positioned by team leadership as a temporal-displacement specialist, leveraging both his Quantum Realm survivor-experience (canonical via the *Children's Crusade* return mechanism and the subsequent Microverse arcs) and his engineering background. He performs well. He does not seek credit. He is, in surveillance terms, *useful and quiet* — the team's reliable middle-of-the-bench veteran.

Granular pattern observations from this period:

- **Combat micro-style has stabilized into a recognizable repertoire**: opening with a giant-form distraction, dropping to insect-scale for the actual mission-critical work, ending with a re-emergence at human scale to extract or de-escalate. The pattern is conservative — he no longer experiments mid-fight the way he did in the Spencer years. Veteran's economy.
- **Verbal tic in mission-brief settings**: he prefixes substantive contributions with "this is probably stupid, but —". Documented in at least seven separate panel-instances across the period. The phrase is a pre-emptive shame-buffer. It is also, increasingly, ignored by teammates who have learned that what follows is usually correct.
- **Eating pattern**: irregular. The subject skips meals when absorbed in workshop tasks and then over-eats reflexively, usually fast food, late, alone. Body composition reflects this — soft midsection, lean limbs, the silhouette of a man whose physical maintenance is incidental to his work rather than its object. He does not weight-train beyond functional minimums. He does cardio to outrun his own thoughts.
- **Social media**: a dormant personal account, last meaningful post several years old. An active Ant-Man Security Solutions account he runs himself, conspicuously folksy in tone, replies to every customer comment within twenty-four hours. The customer-service voice is bright, generous, and slightly performative. The personal voice is silent.
- **Devices**: still two phones. The civilian Android is now upgraded one generation. The pediatric-cardiology billing office is still a frequent contact. The debt is presumably nearly retired but he has not closed the account; it is now ritual.

---

## 4.6 — Current Domestic and Operational Status

**Residence (primary)**: a modest two-bedroom in a working-class corridor of one of the outer boroughs (the canon has moved him out of Avengers Mountain quartering as of the most recent appearances). Second bedroom is nominally Cassie's; she has slept there perhaps four times. It is kept made.

**Residence (secondary)**: a small workshop-office for Ant-Man Security Solutions, separate address, walk-up. He works there mornings and early afternoons. The workshop contains: a tools bench, a sleeping cot he denies using, a coffee maker, an under-counter mini-fridge stocked with off-brand soda, a corkboard with active job notes, and — the only personal item — the taped photograph in the locker.

**Operational status**: reserve Avenger, called in for specialty work and major crises. Not on a permanent active roster. He prefers it this way. Income: combination of a modest Avengers retainer and the Security Solutions revenue; the latter is small but steady and, for the first time in his life, *clean.*

**Vehicular**: a used pickup, second-hand, kept impeccable. He maintains it himself. The cleanliness of the truck is one of the few areas where the subject permits himself visible competence-display.

**Daily route, typical**:
- 06:30 — wake (sleep onset usually around 02:00; total sleep 4–5 hours, fragmented).
- 06:45 — coffee, standing at the kitchen counter, not seated.
- 07:15 — drive to workshop.
- 07:45–13:00 — billable work.
- 13:00 — lunch, almost always taken at one of three rotating cheap counter-service establishments within a six-block radius. He tips heavily. Servers know him.
- 13:30–17:00 — billable work continues, or Avengers consult work if active.
- Evenings — variable. If Cassie is in town, dinner with her, the most stable feature of his week and the one he will cancel any other commitment for. If she is not, workshop hours stretch.
- Late night — workshop, or insomniac tinkering at home, or (rarely) a bar where he nurses one drink for two hours and leaves.

**Relational status**: no current romantic attachment. Has had two brief involvements in the current period, both ended amicably and on his initiative, both terminated at approximately the point where the partner began discussing cohabitation. The Cassie-cathexis still crowds the available bandwidth. He is aware of this. He does not present as actively lonely; he presents as a man who has organized his solitude around a structure he understands.

**Mentor figures, current**: Pym is intermittently re-entered into canon and remains the load-bearing reference; Stark relations are complicated by Stark's own discontinuities; Rogers, when present, remains a quiet north-star figure to whom the subject defers reflexively. *He has not, in 45 years of canon, ever told any of these figures the full extent of his self-assessment.*

**Mentee figures, current**: Cassie (no longer accepts the framing, but he still privately holds it); the Young Avengers veterans in their incidental crossings; informally, almost any young hero in any shared scene — he gravitates, advises lightly, retreats before being asked anything binding.

---

## 4.7 — Current Psychological State (Standing Assessment)

The subject is, at the present moment of the file, in the most stable configuration of his adult life. *Stable does not mean healed.*

The stability is **structural, not resolved**: he has organized his environment to minimize the activation conditions of his core template. Modest income removes acute financial pressure. Reduced ambition removes the over-extension trap. The cautious Cassie-reconciliation provides relational ballast without forcing the dangerous conversation. Reserve Avenger status delivers crisis-discharge opportunities — and recall that he is *healthier in emergencies* — at a survivable frequency. Self-incarceration in 2017 demonstrated, retrospectively, that he had finally internalized at least one part of the mentor-grace template (the punishment) even if he has not internalized the other (the deserving).

What has *not* changed across this period:
- The 0.7-second latency before he speaks Cassie's name.
- The negative core schema. He still believes he is a man held aloft by other people's mercy.
- The "this is probably stupid, but —" pre-buffer.
- The placement of the photograph behind a closing door.
- The pediatric-cardiology billing account, kept open beyond function.
- The fundamental belief that the 1979 Pym-grace was a gift rather than a verdict.

**Risk profile, current**: low-to-moderate. The pattern remains armed. The activation conditions remain specific (financial crisis + Cassie-threat + opportunity). In their absence the subject functions well, generously, and with the unshowy decency that has always been his ground-state. In their presence, even now, the file's expectation is that the template would fire again — perhaps with greater self-awareness this time, perhaps with a longer pause before the rationalization engages, but fire.

**The one intervention that would matter**, as noted in the standing formulation, remains unattempted and unsought: a direct, witnessed, *believed* statement — from Pym, ideally, but from any of the load-bearing mentors — that the grace extended in 1979 was a recognition of what he had already shown himself to be, not a gift bestowed on someone undeserving. He has been paying interest, for forty-five published years, on a debt that was never owed. He is, currently, paying it down quietly, in small honest jobs and in restrained fatherhood and in the careful avoidance of the conditions that would re-open it.

It is, in its way, a kind of grace he is finally extending to himself. He would deny that framing if it were offered to him. He would deflect with humor. There would be a 0.7-second pause first.

— END SECTION —


## Medical History

# UATU DOSSIER — SCOTT EDWARD HARRIS LANG
## Section 3: MEDICAL HISTORY
### File Status: Longitudinal somatic record, 1979–present. Compiled from observable canon, inferred clinical extrapolation, and behavioral signatures consistent with documented physiological events.

---

## 3.1 CONSTITUTIONAL BASELINE

Subject presents as a Caucasian male, approximately 5'10", build oscillating between 165–180 lbs across the publication record depending on era — leaner in incarceration phases (carceral diet, exercise-yard conditioning), heavier and softer in stable domestic intervals (notably the early Miami Ant-Man Security Solutions period, where weight gain is visually depicted alongside the small-business stress arc). Right-handed. Brown hair, brown eyes, light beard growth that he keeps stubbled-down rather than clean-shaven for most of the published record — a low-maintenance grooming choice consistent with both depressive baseline (effort-minimization) and the practical reality of a man who has spent significant time without reliable shaving access.

No documented congenital conditions. No childhood medical events of canonical record. Subject's pre-incarceration baseline must be reconstructed from negative space: he completed an electronics engineering degree, held a position at Stark International, and married — none of which is compatible with a significant chronic illness history. He enters the record as a physiologically healthy adult man whose subsequent medical file is almost entirely *acquired*.

Blood type: not canonical; AB+ inferred from compatibility with broad transfusion needs given his injury frequency, but this is speculation.

Allergies: none documented. Vaccination status presumed current through Stark employment medical and later Avengers medical protocols.

---

## 3.2 OBSTETRIC/PATERNAL MEDICAL CONTEXT — THE CASSIE VARIABLE

The single most clinically significant fact in Lang's medical file is not a fact about his own body. It is the congenital cardiac condition of his daughter, Cassandra Eleanor Lang, identified in early childhood. Subject has lived continuously since approximately 1979 under the conditions of *anticipatory pediatric medical grief*: a parent of a child whose survival is conditional on continuous specialist intervention.

The clinical impact on Subject is multifold and durable:

- **Hypervigilance toward bodily fragility in loved ones.** Subject scans Cassie compulsively for symptoms — pallor, breath quality, fatigue cues — to a degree that, were she not actually ill, would constitute pathological enmeshment. Because she *is* actually ill, the vigilance is rational, but the underlying neurological adaptation persists even in periods of her stable health and generalizes to other children in his care (Future Foundation cohort).
- **Catastrophizing schema around medical events.** Any reported symptom is metabolized as potential terminal collapse. This is the cognitive substrate that makes him recruitable for expedient illegality the moment a medical bill arrives.
- **A learned, durable association between *medical necessity* and *moral compromise*.** This is the single most consequential medical fact in his psychological file. The original burglary that produces Ant-Man is medically motivated. Every recurrence of the pattern is medically rationalized. His somatic-moral economy is fundamentally medicalized.
- **Sleep disruption in pediatric-crisis intervals.** Inferred from behavioral record — Lang shows up to operations sleep-deprived during Cassie-medical arcs, with associated micro-errors he otherwise does not commit.

---

## 3.3 INCARCERATION-PERIOD MEDICAL HISTORY

**First sentence:** New York State penitentiary, post-Vistacorp burglary. Duration: roughly three years served on a longer sentence.

Carceral medical exposures, in order of clinical significance:

- **Chronic sleep architecture disruption.** Block noise, lighting cycles, vigilance-states-in-sleep — these produce durable changes in REM distribution and arousal thresholds that do not fully revert post-release. Lang's adult sleep, where observable in the record, is shallow, easily interrupted, and oriented toward the door. He wakes at sounds civilians do not register. He sleeps poorly the first night in any new environment. He sleeps better in cramped spaces than open ones — a carceral adaptation that civilian observers misread as eccentricity.
- **Threat-appraisal recalibration.** Carceral environments train the amygdala to read posture, gait, and proximity at sub-second latency. This persists. Lang reads rooms faster than his stated background should permit; he does not advertise this skill.
- **Authority-relations conditioning.** Reflexive subordinate posture in the presence of uniformed authority — chin slightly down, hands visible, voice register softened — which he is sometimes aware of and sometimes not.
- **Probable dental compromise.** Carceral dentistry is universally substandard; subject's bite mechanics and likely posterior caries history are inferred but undocumented.
- **Probable subclinical malnutrition during intake periods.** Reversible.
- **Sexual-violence exposure status: undetermined.** Canon does not address. Behavioral record shows no overt PTSD signature specific to assault trauma, but the absence of evidence is not evidence of absence; subject is exactly the demographic to underreport and exactly the personality (humor-armored) to never name it. File-flag, no determination.

**Second sentence:** Miami, post–Power Broker arc. Shorter custodial period. Re-activates and compounds all of the above; the second incarceration is psychologically more damaging than the first because it confirms the recursive structure of his life.

---

## 3.4 PYM PARTICLE EXPOSURE — CUMULATIVE PHYSIOLOGICAL RECORD

Subject has undergone subatomic-scale size shifts intermittently for the bulk of his adult life. This is, in the in-universe canon, a non-trivial physiological insult of poorly characterized long-term sequelae.

**Acute physiological events per shift:**
- Mass-displacement transfer (the Pym Particle reduces apparent size while preserving mass — Lang at ant-scale retains adult human mass, which is the basis of his striking power). The proprioceptive disorientation of this is severe on first exposures and habituates over time. Lang's first weeks with the suit, per the Michelinie/Layton canon, show characteristic vertigo and balance-recovery behaviors.
- Cardiovascular load: the shift itself appears to impose transient tachycardia and blood-pressure spike, inferred from depicted recovery posture.
- Respiratory: at ant-scale, oxygen exchange efficiency is altered; Lang is observed to fatigue faster than scale-mechanics would predict, suggesting subclinical respiratory cost per shift.
- Thermoregulation: surface-area-to-volume ratio collapses at small scale; he should be losing body heat at catastrophic rates and does not, which suggests the Particle itself buffers thermal exchange. Mechanism unknown.

**Cumulative neurological exposure:** Pym himself, in canon, presents documented psychiatric sequelae attributed in part to Particle exposure (the Yellowjacket dissociative episode being the apex example). Lang has not manifested equivalent psychotic-spectrum decompensation. Three competing hypotheses:

1. *Lower cumulative dose.* Lang uses the suit less compulsively than Pym and at less extreme scales. Plausible but incomplete.
2. *Constitutional resilience.* Lang's pre-morbid personality is more integrated than Pym's and absorbs the insult better. Plausible.
3. *Equivalent insult, different expression.* The neurological cost may be expressing itself in his actual symptom profile — the cognitive narrowing under stress, the dissociative flippancy about his own death, the mild derealization features — rather than in frank psychosis. **This is the formulation UATU favors.** Lang may be paying the Pym tax in a different currency.

**Microverse / Quantum-scale exposures:** Subatomic-scale traversals are the highest-risk Particle uses. Each constitutes an exposure to environments outside the validated parameters of human neurology. Long-term cognitive risk is unknown but should be presumed nonzero. Subject does not undergo post-exposure neurological monitoring; no Avengers protocol exists for this.

**Tinnitus.** High probability, undocumented. Communication with ants at ant-scale (technologically mediated through the helmet) and proximity to scale-shift acoustic phenomena should produce chronic high-frequency hearing damage. Subject would normalize and not report.

---

## 3.5 COMBAT INJURY LEDGER

Across forty-five publication years of intermittent costumed activity, Subject has accrued the injury profile of a B-tier frontline operator who avoids the worst hits through scale-evasion but absorbs significant cumulative damage.

**Documented or strongly inferred:**
- Multiple concussive events. Helmet provides protection but is not a sealed combat helmet; he has been struck, thrown, and crushed at scale. Probable subclinical CTE risk in late-career projection.
- Fractures: ribs (multiple, recurrent — high-velocity grabs at insect scale produce thoracic compression injuries when he returns to full size mid-grip); left ulna (inferred); nasal bone (twice minimum, healed slightly asymmetric).
- Lacerations: numerous, distributed. Notable scar on the left forearm from an early-career incident, visible in civilian-dress depictions.
- Burns: minor to moderate, from electronics work as much as from combat. Right hand dorsum shows old solder-burn pattern.
- Soft-tissue: chronic low-grade rotator cuff irritation (right, dominant), consistent with repeated impact-bracing.
- Lower back: chronic. Mass-displacement physics impose unusual loading on the lumbar spine; he carries the stiffness of a man ten years older than he is.
- Hand-and-finger fine-motor: preserved, critical for his engineering work, and he protects it consciously.

**Pain management:** No canonical opioid exposure of concern. Subject is notably *not* a pain-complainer — carceral conditioning plus paternal-stoicism schema produce systematic underreporting of his own discomfort. He will work through injuries that should have him benched.

---

## 3.6 DEATH AND RESURRECTION

**Event:** Atomization at the Avengers Mansion, *Avengers Disassembled* (2004). Mechanism: reality-distortion via Scarlet Witch decompensation event; proximate cause, Kree warship explosion. Subject was killed instantly; no suffering interval of clinical relevance.

**Resurrection:** *Children's Crusade* (2010–12). Mechanism: reality-alteration by Wiccan. Subject restored with apparent physiological continuity from the moment-prior-to-death; no documented somatic deficits attributable to the resurrection itself.

**Clinical impact:** Resurrection trauma has no validated nosology. Behavioral evidence in Subject post-restoration includes:
- **Mild derealization episodes**, particularly when conversation touches on the death itself or on the period during which he did not exist.
- **Dissociative flippancy** — Subject jokes about being dead, references it in casual conversation, deploys it as humor-armor. This is *not* integration; it is distancing. A man who had genuinely processed his own death would not be able to make it a punchline so reliably.
- **Subtle altered relationship to mortality risk.** Post-resurrection, Subject takes physical risks slightly more readily, with a flatter affect about the risk-calculus. The internal price of his own death has been pre-paid in his somatic accounting and the receipt is faded.
- **No reported nightmares of the death event.** This is itself suspicious — either suppressed, dissociated, or genuinely absent because the death was experientially instantaneous. Probable suppression.

The resurrection is the medical event in Lang's file that medical frameworks are least equipped to address. No clinician has ever treated it. No protocol exists.

---

## 3.7 SECONDARY BEREAVEMENT — CASSIE'S DEATH

The killing of Cassie by Doom in the same arc that restored Lang is, somatically, the most damaging event in his life. Bereavement of a child produces measurable, durable changes in immune function, cardiovascular risk, sleep, and cortisol regulation. Lang during the Future Foundation period shows:

- Weight fluctuation (loss during acute phase, slow regain).
- Compromised sleep, masked by overwork.
- Increased baseline cortisol inferred from behavioral signatures (irritability uncharacteristic of him, somatic complaints he dismisses).
- Sublimated grief expressed through hyperprotective custodianship of the FF children.

Cassie's eventual restoration in canon does not somatically undo this. Subject lived the loss. The cellular record of the loss remains. He is a bereaved parent in his body even after the metaphysics resolves the bereavement.

---

## 3.8 SUBSTANCE USE

**Alcohol:** Social use. Beer-predominant. No canonical pattern consistent with use disorder. Notable for its absence given stressor load — most men with his biography would be drinking more. Two protective factors are inferred: (a) carceral exposure to active alcoholism in others produced an aversion model; (b) compulsive behavior in Subject expresses through *action* rather than *ingestion* — he discharges pressure by doing illegal things, not by drinking.

**Tobacco:** No record.

**Cannabis:** No record. Plausible occasional use given era and demographic, undocumented.

**Stimulants / opioids / sedatives:** No documented use. No prescription record of psychotropic medication of any kind, which is itself a clinical finding — Subject has never been offered, or has never accepted, pharmacological support for a symptom profile that arguably warrants it. The likely vector is *avoidance of psychiatric contact*, which a man with two felony convictions and a security-clearance-adjacent superhero career has rational reasons to maintain.

**Caffeine:** Heavy. Coffee-predominant. Functional dependency, undiagnosed, untreated, unremarkable.

---

## 3.9 SENSORY AND NEUROLOGICAL STATUS

- **Vision:** Functionally normal. Mild presbyopia age-appropriate; uses readers for fine electronics work and is mildly embarrassed by them.
- **Hearing:** Probable bilateral high-frequency loss from Particle-shift acoustic exposure and combat concussive history. Undiagnosed. Subject reads lips slightly more than he should need to and occasionally mishears in crowded rooms.
- **Proprioception:** *Above baseline.* Decades of scale-shifting have produced a recalibrated body-schema that is unusually plastic. Subject orients in three-dimensional space — including unfamiliar architectures — faster than untrained civilians. He does not consciously notice this.
- **Vestibular:** Robust. Has habituated to extreme acceleration changes most humans never experience.
- **Cognitive baseline:** Preserved. High engineering-analytical capacity, intact verbal fluency, intact memory. Stress-bound attentional narrowing as described in the psychological section is *motivated*, not organic.

---

## 3.10 PSYCHOLOGICAL IMPACT — INTEGRATIVE NOTE

The medical history of this Subject cannot be parsed as separate from his psychology because the somatic and the moral are, in his case, the same circuit. The cardiac fragility of his daughter is what made him a thief. The carceral experience of his thievery is what calibrated his nervous system to authority. The acceptance of the Pym suit is what installed the mentor-grace template that governs every subsequent decision. The atomization and resurrection are what gave him the dissociative humor that now functions as his most reliable defense. The bereavement of his daughter, however metaphysically reversed, is what produced the protective-custodian character he is in midlife.

He is a man whose body has been the site of: chronic anticipatory medical grief, two incarcerations, decades of unvalidated subatomic exposure, a death, a resurrection, the death of a child, and the restoration of that child. He has never received psychiatric care, has never been on a medication, has never undergone a neurological workup post-Pym exposure, has never been screened for CTE, has never had his hearing tested, has never spoken to anyone, on the record, about being dead.

The medical file is, in this sense, a file of *what has happened to him that no one has ever treated.* He is carrying the entire load uncatalogued.

That, in itself, is the diagnosis.

— END SECTION 3 —


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS: SCOTT EDWARD HARRIS LANG

## File Subsection 7.4 — Bodily Record, Cross-Indexed by State
### Compiled from longitudinal observation, 1979–present canon. All entries derive from documented behavioral panels and inferential extension consistent with same.

---

## 7.4.1 — Baseline Anthropometry & Build

Subject presents at approximately 5'11", 175 lb at his stable weight, with a build that reads as *engineer-who-was-once-fit* rather than *combatant*. Shoulders broader than the torso would predict — an inheritance, possibly, of upper-body work during his first incarceration where carceral routine reliably produces a press-and-pull silhouette without proportional lower-body development. Calves and forearms underdeveloped relative to chest and deltoids. Posture in repose has a forward-rounded shoulder line — the body of a man who spent years bent over circuit boards and then years bent over a prison mattress.

Resting body composition fluctuates by era. In stable Avengers-tenure periods he carries an additional eight to ten pounds, soft around the midsection, the body of a divorced father who eats convenience food. In Miami-era (Spencer run) he is leaner, sun-darker, but the leanness is stress-leanness, not training-leanness — visible in the slight gauntness around the temples and the way his belt sits at a different notch.

Hair: dark brown, going to grey at the temples by the FF period, kept short and uncomplicated. Self-cuts when money is tight (Miami era — visible asymmetry at the sideburns in surveillance-adjacent panels). When solvent, defaults to a $15 walk-in cut, never barbered. Facial hair: erratic. Clean-shaven in employment periods; three-to-five-day stubble in transitional periods; nothing approaching a designed beard, ever. He does not curate his face.

---

## 7.4.2 — Gait & Locomotion

**Walking baseline:** medium-short stride, weight slightly forward, hands often partly in pockets — a *contained* walk, designed to occupy minimal sidewalk. He moves like a man who has been told to keep his hands visible and has compromised by keeping them visible-adjacent. The walk is not furtive; it is *minimizing*. He does not swing his arms fully.

**Stairs:** taken two at a time when alone and unobserved (the body still wants to move quickly); one at a time, with a hand on the rail, when accompanied by Cassie or by a senior figure. The deference is somatic.

**Approaching a door:** habitual half-second pause before entering any room he has not entered before. The pause looks like he is checking his phone or adjusting his cuff; it is actually a threat-assessment learned in custody. Persistent across every era post-incarceration.

**Running:** efficient, slightly pigeon-toed under fatigue, arms held lower than is biomechanically optimal — a runner who learned to run carrying something (a child, a bag, a stolen object). He is faster than he looks for the first forty yards and slower than he looks past two hundred.

**At size-shift:** the body's proprioceptive reset on returning to standard scale produces a characteristic full-body shudder-and-shake, like a dog leaving water. He has done this thousands of times. It is now invisible to him and immediate to any observer. He often follows the shudder with a single hand-to-sternum touch, a sensorimotor check that the heart is where it should be.

---

## 7.4.3 — Hand Behavior

Hands are the most informationally dense region of the subject. They are large for his frame, with the slightly knobbed knuckles of an electronics technician who has bashed his hands inside server cabinets for two decades, and a small white scar across the dorsum of the left hand (origin uncatalogued; probably workshop, probably 1980s).

**Resting position:** hands prefer to be *doing something*. Default fidgets, in observed frequency:

1. Wedding-ring-absence touch. The left ring finger receives a thumb-pad stroke roughly once every four to six minutes when seated and idle. The ring has been gone for decades. The gesture has not gone with it.
2. Pen-spinning. Single rotation, between index and middle finger, repeated. Engineer's tic.
3. Coin-walking across knuckles — learned in custody, retained for life. Emerges specifically when waiting for news about Cassie.
4. Picking at the cuticle of the right thumb. Stress-bound. The cuticle is chronically ragged.
5. Adjustment of the watch (always worn on the left wrist, always a cheap digital or a midrange analog, never expensive even when he can afford expensive — money on his wrist would feel like a lie).

**Under stress:** hands migrate to the back of the neck, palm flat, fingers spread, in a self-soothing nape-clasp. He will hold this for three to eight seconds, then release with an audible exhale. This gesture predicts a difficult sentence by approximately two seconds.

**Under threat (combat-imminent):** hands drop to mid-thigh, slightly behind the hip-line, fingers loose and ready. The drop is the tell. Anyone who has fought him more than twice has learned to read it.

**Intimate / affectionate:** with Cassie specifically — the right hand goes to the crown of her head, palm cupped, regardless of her age. He has done this since she was three. He does it to her at sixteen. He will do it to her at thirty. The gesture has not updated. With romantic partners, by contrast, his hands are tentative, often held just-not-touching for a beat too long before contact — asking permission the body never voiced.

---

## 7.4.4 — Facial Repertoire

**Default expression in repose:** a faint, asymmetric upward pull at the right corner of the mouth — not quite a smile, a *readiness* for one. This is the social-camouflage face. It signals approachability, and it is on by default because he has learned that an unsmiling ex-con face is read as threat.

**Genuine smile:** broad, gum-revealing, eye-crinkling, briefly lowers the head. Rare. Cassie produces it reliably; Hank Pym produced it twice on record; a successful microscale infiltration produces it; praise from a senior hero produces it followed within two seconds by a deflection.

**Listening face:** mouth slightly open, head canted approximately fifteen degrees right, eyebrows raised. He looks, when listening, like he is being told something he doesn't quite believe but wants to. This is genuine — he is metabolizing in real time — and it makes him a disarming interlocutor.

**Lying face:** the asymmetric mouth-pull becomes symmetric. The smile *evens out*. This is the one reliable tell. He believes he is a good liar; he is not, because his face becomes *more* composed than baseline under deception, and composure is uncharacteristic.

**Under interrogation by authority:** the eyebrows lift fractionally and stay lifted. He learned in custody that raised eyebrows read as cooperative. He cannot consciously suppress this any more than he can suppress a knee-jerk.

**Micro-tells:**
- A two-blink cluster precedes any statement beginning "I just need to —". This is the rationalization opener and the blink-cluster is the conscience flagging it.
- A tongue-press against the inside of the left cheek when he is being praised. Discomfort-bound.
- A nose-wrinkle, brief, when Cassie's name is spoken by someone who does not know her well. Protective.
- The right eye narrows slightly more than the left when he is calculating. Visible during any tactical assessment.

---

## 7.4.5 — Voice & Speech

Mid-tenor, slight residual New York consonant-shaping under stress (the *coffee* vowel, the dropped *r* at sentence-end), otherwise generalized American. Volume is consistently below the room's median — he undertalks. People lean in to hear him, which he has learned is socially useful.

**Speech rate:** moderate baseline, accelerating under stress. He develops a characteristic *sentence-stacking* under pressure, where he begins the next sentence before finishing the previous, the second sentence functioning as a softener for the first. ("I know how it looks, I just — listen, I had to —")

**Filler pattern:** "look," "listen," and "the thing is" cluster around moments of self-justification. "Honestly" precedes the least honest sentences. Frequency of "honestly" is inversely correlated with truth-content over a longitudinal sample.

**Laughter:** a short, exhaled *huh* — single syllable, often self-directed. Genuine laughter is a longer four-syllable cascade that ends in a wheeze. The wheeze is diagnostic of genuine versus performed amusement.

**Silence:** uncomfortable with it. Fills it. The only person around whom he can sit silent is Cassie. With everyone else, including senior heroes, he will produce a sentence within seven to nine seconds of a conversational gap.

---

## 7.4.6 — Eye Behavior & Gaze

**Default gaze pattern:** distributed scan — he looks at faces, but also at exits, hands, and ceiling corners, in a cycling pattern roughly every four seconds. This is a carceral residue and has not faded across decades. In any new room he will locate the exits within his first thirty seconds and reassess them every two to three minutes thereafter.

**Eye contact in conversation:** good, slightly over-good — he holds it a beat longer than the norm, which reads as sincerity and is partly that and partly an overcorrection learned during parole and reentry, where avoidance was read as guilt.

**Eye contact with authority figures:** *worse* than baseline. He glances down and to the left when addressed by Captain America or Reed Richards. The mentor introjection produces somatic deference.

**Eye contact with Cassie:** softens fully. The scan stops. She is the only stimulus that overrides the perimeter-check reflex.

**Threat-state pupils:** dilate visibly. Subject is one of those individuals whose autonomic response is anatomically legible at conversational distance.

---

## 7.4.7 — Posture & Seated Behavior

**Standing:** asymmetric weight distribution, slightly more on the right foot, left knee subtly bent. A relaxed but ready-to-move stance. He does not stand *at attention* even when nominally required to.

**Seated, civilian context:** forward lean, elbows on knees, hands clasped or fidgeting between them. The body of a man waiting to be called into an office. He does this in his own kitchen.

**Seated, briefing context:** leans back, one ankle crossed over the opposite knee in figure-four position, arms loosely along the chair-back. *Performs* casual to compensate for the deference his face is leaking.

**Seated, with Cassie:** body angled fifteen to twenty degrees toward her, regardless of room geometry. He orients his torso toward her like a plant to light. Unconscious.

**Sleep posture:** side-sleeper, right side, knees drawn slightly up, one hand under the pillow. Carceral. The hand under the pillow is a residue of needing to know where his hand was when he woke. He has slept this way for forty-plus years and will not sleep otherwise; on missions in shared quarters he will fake supine sleep until others are out, then turn.

---

## 7.4.8 — Sleep Architecture

Approximately five to six hours per night in stable periods; four to five in stress periods; binge-sleeps ten to twelve hours on the first day after a mission as a recovery dump. Sleep-onset is fast (carceral training: you slept when you could) but sleep-maintenance is poor. Two to three nocturnal wakings is baseline. The first waking, between 0230 and 0330, is the *Cassie waking* — he reaches for the phone, checks for messages, does not return to sleep for thirty to ninety minutes.

Dreams, where reported: prison dreams (recurrent, decade-stable), the *can't-find-Cassie* dream (recurrent, intensified post-Disassembled), and a specific Microverse dream involving the inability to return to size. He does not discuss these. Sleep talks occasionally — single-word, usually her name.

Naps: takes them readily, anywhere, often in armored vehicles or QuinJets. A skill of the formerly-incarcerated and the chronically-tired father.

---

## 7.4.9 — Eating & Ingestion

Eats fast. Carceral fast. Plate-to-empty in eight to twelve minutes regardless of meal quality. Has worked, in calmer periods, to slow this when eating with Cassie — visible self-pacing, fork put down between bites, often forgotten and picked back up within thirty seconds.

**Food preferences:** comfort-skewed and cost-conscious. Defaults: pizza, takeout Chinese, diner breakfast, supermarket rotisserie chicken. Will eat anything offered without complaint. Does not cook complex meals; produces serviceable pancakes, scrambled eggs, grilled cheese — the dad-with-custody-weekend repertoire, calcified.

**Coffee:** heavy. Four to six cups by noon. Black if he made it; cream and sugar if someone else did, because correcting the offer feels rude.

**Alcohol:** moderate, situational. One to three beers in a social context. Avoids hard liquor, not from any program but from an unarticulated sense that he should not be the kind of man who drinks brown liquor in the afternoon.

**Snacking:** stress-bound. Pretzels, chips, the cheap salt-and-crunch end of the spectrum. Will eat an entire bag without registering it during a tense work period.

**Notable absence:** he does not eat meals alone at a table. Alone, he eats standing at a counter, or on the couch, or in the car. The table is for company. This is a widower-divorcé pattern, possibly also a custodial residue (private meals were not a thing).

---

## 7.4.10 — Grooming & Self-Presentation

**Showering:** fast, functional, daily, with the carceral habit of facing the door. Water temperature: hot, near the top of his tolerance. He has explained this once, deflected, never returned to it.

**Dental:** good, basic, twice-daily, the teeth of a man who could not afford serious cosmetic work and has accepted his slightly imperfect lower row.

**Clothing baseline:** jeans, T-shirt, hoodie or zip-up jacket, sneakers. Inoffensive earth tones and washed-out blues. He owns one sport coat for court appearances and one suit for weddings and funerals, both slightly out of date. He does not shop; he replaces.

**Specific items of unusual longevity:** a beaten leather wallet (1990s vintage, visibly creased, replaced only when destroyed); a watch worn until the battery dies twice before replacement; sneakers worn past structural integrity. He is not sentimental about objects in principle but is functionally sentimental in practice — replacement requires a precipitating event.

**Smell:** generic soap, generic detergent, no cologne. Faintly machine-shop in the workshop, faintly hot-electronics after suit use.

---

## 7.4.11 — Sexuality & Romantic Somatics

The most underdeveloped region of the file. Subject's sexual life is, by superhero-cohort standards, conspicuously low-volume and low-investment.

**Approach pattern:** slow, indirect, deferential. Does not initiate. Reads cues conservatively and often misses available ones. The pattern is consistent with a man whose libidinal economy is over-mortgaged to the paternal cathexis and whose self-concept does not include "desirable."

**In bed (inferential):** considerate, attentive, anxious-to-please, likely under-asks-for. The same conflict-avoidance that governs his civilian relationships will govern intimate negotiation. Will fall asleep quickly afterward — exhaustion is real, but also exit.

**Post-coital pattern:** the side-sleep posture engages immediately. He does not stay turned toward the partner past the first ten to twenty minutes. This is not rejection; it is the body returning to its trained configuration.

**Avoidance markers:** he does not keep partners' belongings in his living space past a certain threshold. He does not display photographs of romantic partners. Cassie's photograph is everywhere; no one else's is anywhere.

---

## 7.4.12 — State-Shift Differentials

The same body reads differently across four states. The differential is the diagnostic.

**CALM (rare, sustained only in low-stakes Cassie-time):** shoulders drop nearly an inch. The asymmetric mouth-readiness softens into actual rest. Hands quiet. Scan-rate halves. Voice drops in pitch. He looks, in this state, ten years younger than his calendar age.

**STRESS (chronic baseline in financial-precarity arcs):** shoulders rise, neck shortens visibly. Cuticle-picking accelerates. Nape-clasps cluster. Speech-stacking begins. Sleep degrades. Snacking increases. Sentence-opening "honestly" frequency doubles. He becomes, paradoxically, *more* charming — the surface deploys harder to mask the substrate.

**THREAT (combat imminent or active):** the entire postural economy reorganizes. Shoulders drop *because they have to*, hands fall to thigh-line, scan-rate triples and tightens, peripheral vision engages, breathing deepens and slows, voice drops half an octave and loses all filler. He becomes briefly the man he believes he is not — competent, calm, lethal-when-needed, decisive. Then the threat resolves and the body reassembles its civilian compromise within ninety seconds.

**INTIMACY (with Cassie, almost exclusively):** the perimeter-check shuts off. Torso orients. Right hand seeks the crown of her head. Eye contact stabilizes and softens. Voice slows. He becomes, for the duration of the contact, congruent — face and body and word doing the same thing. It is the only state in which this is reliably true.

The dossier's central somatic finding: **Subject's body tells the truth his self-concept will not.** The competence is there, in the gait under threat and the hand under fire; the love is there, in the orientation toward his daughter; the wound is there, in the carceral residues he has never shed. He is, bodily, a more coherent man than he believes himself to be. The gap between the body's testimony and the self's testimony is the entire pathology.

— END SUBSECTION 7.4 —


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 7
## ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS
### Subject: Scott Edward Harris Lang
### Cross-reference: §3 (Psychological), §4 (Psychiatric), §5 (Personality)

---

## 7.1 Attachment Classification & Origins

The subject's attachment organization is **anxious-preoccupied with a vertically-stratified relational geometry**. He does not relate to other human beings on a flat plane; he sorts them, almost reflexively, into one of three tiers — *those above him* (mentors, authorities, betters), *those below him* (children, mentees, the protected), and *those beside him* (peers) — and his functional capacity declines sharply as one moves from the first two categories into the third. Peer intimacy is the weakest axis of his relational life. He has spent forty-five published years building careers around men he calls *sir* in his head and children he would die for, and has produced almost no enduring lateral friendships of equal weight.

The origin of this geometry is not difficult to triangulate. The biographical record gives us a father (Lang Sr., minimally drawn but consistently characterized as disappointed in Scott's choices, distant in affect, conditional in approval), an early professional life under Tony Stark — an authority figure who fires him, then *re-hires him after prison*, establishing the foundational adult template — and the catalytic Pym encounter, in which the subject expects punishment from a superior and receives instead a *bequest*. The Pym moment is not merely an event in his life; it is the **organizing schema** of his entire adult relational system. Every authority figure thereafter is implicitly tested against the Pym template: *Will you punish me as I deserve, or will you, against expectation, vouch for me?* He does not consciously stage this test. He simply behaves in ways that make it inevitable.

The Cassie-attachment is structurally separate from this hierarchy and must be addressed first, because every other relational pattern in the file is partly a deflection from, or sublimation of, this one bond.

---

## 7.2 The Cassie Bond — Primary Attachment Object

There is no other relationship in the subject's life that competes with this one for emotional bandwidth, and it is critical to file accuracy to understand that this is **not healthy parental devotion** in the ordinary sense. It is a *singular cathexis* of the kind clinicians associate with anxious-preoccupied caregivers in whom an early traumatic loss has fused parental love with existential terror. Cassie's congenital heart condition installed, before the original burglary, a permanent state of anticipatory grief; the subject has never had a relationship with his daughter that was not also a relationship with her potential death. The original crime was committed under this pressure. Her actual death in *Children's Crusade* and his own intervening death produced a relationship now textured by **mutual resurrection** — neither of them is supposed to be alive, both know it, neither discusses it.

Behavioral markers across the longitudinal record:

- **Information asymmetry as love-language.** The subject systematically withholds from Cassie the parts of his life that would disappoint her. This is not deception in the antisocial sense — it is *protective dissociation* of his self-image as her father from his self-image as a recidivist. He cannot tolerate her seeing both at once. The Spencer run makes this explicit: every Power Broker job is followed by an evasive Cassie call.
- **Compensatory presence.** When physically with her, he over-corrects: too attentive, too generative of small rituals, too willing to drop other commitments. The presence is qualitatively *anxious-attentive*, not relaxed-attentive — he is monitoring her constantly for signs that something is wrong.
- **Avoidance of confrontation.** The relationship's eventual rupture in the Spencer arc was preceded by *years* of small evasions that should have been small conversations. He cannot deliver bad news to Cassie. He waits, and waits, until the bad news delivers itself, and then collapses.
- **Identification.** He projects himself onto her in characteristic anxious-preoccupied fashion — her independence reads to him as rejection, her hero career reads to him as critique of his (*she became what I am supposed to be*), her friendships with the Young Avengers register as substitute paternity from which he is excluded. He does not name any of this. He jokes around it.

The Cassie bond is the load-bearing structure of his personality and the **single point of failure** of every other relational system. When it is stable, he is stable. When it is threatened, every defense from §3 engages simultaneously and his judgment collapses.

---

## 7.3 Vertical Bonds Upward — The Mentor Pattern

The subject forms attachments to authority figures with unusual speed, unusual depth, and unusual durability. Pym, Stark, Reed Richards, Captain America, T'Challa during the FF run, and to a lesser degree Jan Van Dyne all occupy this slot at different points. The pattern is consistent enough to be diagnostic:

**Phase 1 — Audition.** Initial contact is marked by exaggerated deference, self-deprecation calibrated to invite correction, and a particular tell — he will name his own criminal record *first*, before the mentor figure has the chance to raise it. This is not honesty for honesty's sake; it is **preemptive surrender of the worst card in his hand** so that the relationship can begin from a position he controls. He cannot tolerate the suspense of waiting for the prison record to surface.

**Phase 2 — Apprentice positioning.** Once accepted, he settles into a deputy posture that is comfortable to him and structurally unstable for the relationship. He will defer on tactical questions where his own judgment is plainly superior. He will accept assignments that under-utilize his engineering competence. He will read the mentor's affect for approval-signals with the attentiveness of a man who has been doing this his whole life — which, the file suggests, he has.

**Phase 3 — Over-extension.** When the mentor extends trust beyond what the subject feels he has earned (which, given his self-concept, is virtually any trust at all), the unearned-feeling weight activates the Pym-grace template. He will then take on additional risk, additional self-sacrifice, additional silent loyalty, to *retroactively justify* the trust. This is the mechanism by which mentors reliably get more out of him than they asked for, and also the mechanism by which he reliably injures himself in their service.

**Phase 4 — Disappointment-aversion.** The subject will avoid honest disagreement with a mentor for as long as humanly possible, and when forced into it, will frame the disagreement apologetically and tentatively even when he is correct. Reed Richards in particular triggers this — the FF run shows Lang routinely deferring to Reed-thinking on questions where his own ground-level judgment was sounder.

**Phase 5 — Rupture or stabilization.** The mentor either dies, leaves, betrays, or — rarely — stays long enough for the subject to begin metabolizing the relationship as something other than tutelage. The Cap relationship is the closest to genuine stabilization. The Pym relationship was permanently scarred by Pym's own deterioration, which the subject experienced as the betrayal of the original gift. He has never fully forgiven Pym for not being the man who gave him the suit.

**The diagnostic point:** he does not need these mentors *tactically*. He is competent, often more competent than they grant. He needs them **structurally** — they are the external regulators of his self-worth. Without one in place, the negative core schema runs unchecked.

---

## 7.4 Vertical Bonds Downward — The Protective Pattern

With younger heroes, children in his charge, and the FF kids in particular, the subject exhibits the **single healthiest relational mode in his entire file**. He is patient, generous, funny without being self-deprecating, attentive without being anxious, and — critically — *willing to be the authority figure he himself never trusted himself to be*. This is sublimation at high function: he becomes for these children what he believed Pym was for him, and in doing so partially repairs the wound of having been (in his own self-narrative) unworthy of it.

Specific markers:

- He does not perform competence for these children; he simply uses it, and lets them see him use it. The defensive self-deprecation drops by an order of magnitude.
- He does not lie to them. The information-asymmetry pattern he runs with Cassie is *absent* with substitute children — possibly because the stakes feel lower, possibly because they are not the load-bearing attachment and so the catastrophic-loss anxiety is muted.
- He physically positions himself between them and danger with no observable hesitation. This is overdetermined — paternal instinct, survivor guilt over Cassie's death, sublimated protective drive — but the behavior is consistent across every iteration.
- He grants them more credit for their own judgment than he grants himself, and considerably more than Pym ever granted him. He is, in this register, the *anti-Pym*.

The Future Foundation era is where this pattern is most legible, and the file should flag that it represents the subject's **highest sustained psychological functioning** in the entire publication record. The implication: structured protective custodianship of substitute children regulates him better than any other configuration of his life. He needs to be needed by the young and not-quite-his.

---

## 7.5 Lateral Bonds — The Peer Deficit

This is the conspicuous gap. The subject has had **no enduring peer friendship of equal emotional weight** to either his mentor bonds or his protective bonds. He maintains cordial colleague-relations with a wide range of heroes — Jen Walters, Clint Barton, Spider-Man, the Wasp — but does not metabolize them as peers. He upward-tilts even with people his own grade.

The mechanism: peer relationships require the subject to occupy a position of *equal worth*, which his core schema does not permit. He cannot sustain the posture. Within a few interactions he will have positioned the peer slightly above him (treating them as a quasi-mentor) or slightly below (treating them as someone to be helped). The flat axis collapses.

The exceptions are instructive. His relationship with Jen Walters has had moments of genuine peer texture, and these correlate with periods where she is herself struggling and so the subject can occupy a *mutual* register — two people each privately convinced they are the screw-up of the friendship. Clint Barton is the other near-peer, and the relationship works for the same reason: another recovering-from-himself ex-criminal-adjacent figure whose self-concept matches Lang's closely enough that the vertical-sorting mechanism does not have material to work with.

Romantic relationships fall into this same deficit and are addressed below.

---

## 7.6 Romantic & Sexual Attachment

The romantic record is **thin, evasive, and tellingly under-developed** across forty-five years. Peggy Rae is the longest-running romantic figure and the relationship is characterized throughout by a peculiar *low-investment* quality on the subject's part — affectionate, decent, present, but never of a depth that competes with the Cassie-cathexis. Other romantic encounters are episodic and similarly muted.

The file's interpretation: the Cassie-attachment occupies the bandwidth that would otherwise be available for adult intimate partnership. He is not asexual, not avoidant in the conventional sense, and not incapable of warmth toward women — he simply does not have the emotional reserves to invest a second primary attachment of comparable weight. To do so would require dilution of the Cassie-cathexis, which his system reads as betrayal of her.

Secondary mechanism: adult intimate partnership demands the *peer-bond* he cannot sustain. A romantic partner cannot be a mentor (functional but pathologized) or a mentee (inappropriate and contrary to his ethics). She must be a peer, and the peer slot is structurally vacant in his geometry. Romantic partners therefore drift, over time, into either *mentor-adjacent* configurations (he defers, asks her judgment on everything, treats her as the regulator of his self-worth) or *protected* configurations (he positions her as someone to be shielded, which she correctly experiences as condescension and a refusal of true intimacy).

He does not cheat. He does not exploit. He does not perform romance. He is, by every available metric, a *decent* partner in the small ways. He is also, by every available metric, *not fully present* — and the women he has been involved with appear to have intuited this and largely chosen to move on.

---

## 7.7 The Trust Architecture — How He Decides Whom to Trust

The subject's trust mechanism is **front-loaded, fast, and poorly defended.** He extends substantial provisional trust on first contact, predicated on a combination of (a) the other person's apparent competence and (b) the other person's willingness to *accept him as he is*, criminal record disclosed up front. People who do not flinch at the disclosure clear the initial threshold instantly, and the subject's defenses against them remain low for an unusually long time.

This is the central vulnerability. **Manipulators recruit him by accepting his self-disclosed worst card and then flattering his competence.** Power Broker is the canonical example — the recruitment runs precisely on this template, and the subject walks into it knowing better at every step. The pattern is repeated often enough in the canon that it must be treated as a stable exploitability, not a one-off lapse in judgment.

He does not extend trust based on shared values, shared history, or institutional affiliation. He extends it based on **felt grace** — does this person treat me as worthy of being treated as worthy? Anyone who can manufacture that signal gets in.

Conversely, he is slow to *withdraw* trust once extended. Betrayal must be repeated and explicit before he will revise downward. The first instance is rationalized (misunderstanding, pressure, mitigating circumstance — he extends to others the rationalizations he extends to himself). The second is acknowledged but minimized. Only by the third does he protect himself, and by then the damage is structural.

---

## 7.8 Distrust, Betrayal, and the Repair Mechanism

When the subject *is* betrayed, the response is characteristic and worth full notation:

**He does not retaliate.** There is no documented instance in the canon of the subject seeking revenge against a betrayer. The closest he comes is operational opposition — he will work against them if they are now an enemy — but the *affect* is not vengeful. It reads more as sorrow.

**He blames himself first.** The reflexive interpretation of any betrayal is *I should have seen it; I let this happen; I trusted wrongly because I am a poor judge.* The other person's agency is granted but minimized. This is the negative core schema doing its work in real time.

**He repairs first.** When he is the *betrayer* — when he has lied to Cassie, evaded a mentor, taken a job he shouldn't have — the repair posture is immediate, abject, and over-apologetic. He will accept disproportionate consequence to clear the moral ledger. He will offer more than is asked. The repair is structured as *restoration of grace* — he is asking, in essence, to be vouched for again. This is the only template he has for resolving relational damage.

**He does not forgive himself.** Even when forgiven by the other party, the subject does not metabolize the resolution. He files it away as another instance of unearned grace, which adds to the cumulative debt he believes he owes the world. This is why repeated cycles of transgression-and-forgiveness do not produce learning. The forgiveness is the *opposite* of corrective feedback — each instance reinforces the original schema rather than disconfirming it.

---

## 7.9 The Master Relational Template

Synthesizing across every category above, the file identifies a single template that the subject repeats in every significant relationship, with variations in surface form:

1. **Approach with disclosed inferiority.** He volunteers the worst of himself first, ostensibly as honesty, functionally as control of the narrative.
2. **Receive provisional acceptance.** The other party either flinches (the relationship truncates) or accepts (the relationship proceeds).
3. **Interpret acceptance as grace, not as judgment-of-worth.** The subject does not update his self-concept upward. He updates his sense of debt to the other party upward.
4. **Over-extend in service of the relationship.** He gives more than is asked, accepts more risk than is required, defers more than is necessary.
5. **Manage information to protect the other party's view of him.** Withhold transgressions, evade hard conversations, present a curated self.
6. **Decompensate under stress in a way that violates the curated presentation.** The hidden transgressions surface; the evasions collapse; the relationship is exposed to the version of him he was hiding.
7. **Accept rupture or beg repair, framed as restoration of grace.** Never as renegotiation of terms. Never as a claim to equal standing.
8. **If repaired, return to step 3 with debt now compounded.**

This loop runs with Pym. It runs with Stark. It runs, in attenuated form, with Cap and Reed. It runs catastrophically with Cassie, where steps 5 and 6 are the engine of the eventual rupture. It runs with Peggy Rae and other romantic partners, where the loop simply attenuates and exits at step 6 without progressing to repair.

**The intervention that would break the loop is identified in §1 of this dossier and bears repetition here:** the subject would need to internalize that the grace extended at step 3 is *not* grace but *recognition* — that the other party is not vouching for him out of charity but out of accurate assessment of his worth. He has never accepted this reframe from any source. He may not be capable of accepting it from any external source; the loop's stability suggests the reframe would have to be generated from within, possibly under conditions of sustained reciprocal honesty with Cassie that the canon has not yet permitted.

---

## 7.10 File Note on Operational Implications

For purposes of total-surveillance utility: the subject is **recruitable, manipulable, and predictable along the lines described above**, and is *least* defended at the points where he believes himself most virtuous (the moment of grace-acceptance, the moment of repair, the moment a mentor figure extends trust). His greatest defensive strength is paradoxically located in acute crisis, where the relational architecture goes offline and pure competence takes over.

He is not a man who can be turned against his own ethical core. He is a man whose ethical core can be *routed around* by anyone who learns the template.

The template has been legible in the published record for forty-five years. The subject himself appears to be the only person in his life who has not read it.

— END SECTION 7 —


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 7
## DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS
### Subject: Lang, Scott Edward Harris

---

## 7.0 Preface — How To Read This Section

The defensive architecture of this subject is unusually legible, which is itself the first finding. Lang's defenses are not brittle, not deeply repressed, and not character-armored in the way a narcissistic or paranoid structure would be. They run close to the surface, they are visible to the subject himself in lucid moments, and several of them double as social presentation. This makes him a *transparent* personality in the technical sense — what you see is most of what is there — but it also means his defenses cannot be stripped without exposing the negative core schema directly, which would decompensate him. The defenses are load-bearing precisely because the building underneath is thin.

What follows is the complete catalogue, ranked from most primitive (developmentally earliest, most reality-distorting) to most mature (developmentally latest, most reality-preserving), per the Vaillant/Perry hierarchy as adapted for behavioral-record reconstruction. Each entry maps the mechanism, its behavioral fingerprint in the record, its specific in-canon triggers, its functional value, and its cost.

---

## 7.1 PRIMITIVE / IMAGE-DISTORTING DEFENSES

These are scarce in Lang's record — diagnostically significant in itself. A subject who has been incarcerated twice, atomized, resurrected, lost a child, and worked under sustained Pym-Particle exposure ought, statistically, to lean harder on splitting, projective identification, or psychotic denial. He does not. The primitive register is present but thin.

### 7.1.1 Mild Dissociative Distancing (sub-clinical)

**Mechanism:** Affective separation from autobiographical content too large to be metabolized in real time.

**Fingerprint:** The flippancy about his own death. Lang refers to having been atomized by the Scarlet Witch in throwaway one-liners — "yeah, that happened" — with a tonal register that does not match the content. This is not bravado and not processed acceptance; it is the verbal signature of an experience that has been *filed* rather than integrated. Similar register appears around Cassie's death in *Children's Crusade* — he speaks about it, but the speaking has a slight glassiness, as though narrated by a man one room over from himself.

**Triggers:** Direct inquiry into death, resurrection, or Cassie's death by a non-intimate. With intimates (Cassie, Pym in his lucid years) the dissociative film thins and grief surfaces unbuffered.

**Function:** Permits continued functioning in environments — superhero work, parenting, employment — where collapsing into the unprocessed material would be catastrophic.

**Cost:** Prevents actual grief work. The material remains live but quarantined; under sufficient stress it leaks as somatic startle, sleep disturbance, and the depressive baseline color noted elsewhere in this file.

### 7.1.2 Denial-in-Action (limited)

**Mechanism:** Behavioral, not cognitive, denial — Lang knows the thing he is about to do is wrong; he proceeds as if the knowing did not occur.

**Fingerprint:** The Power Broker arc. The original 1979 burglary. Multiple smaller episodes in the Spencer run where he takes a job he has correctly identified as compromised and simply acts as though the identification did not happen. The cognitive content is intact — interrogated afterward, he can articulate every reason the choice was wrong. The denial is located in the gap between knowing and acting.

**Function:** Permits the rationalization engine (7.2.1) to operate without intra-psychic friction.

**Cost:** The behavioral record. Two prison sentences. Estrangement from Cassie.

### 7.1.3 Note on absent primitive defenses

He does **not** split (people remain three-dimensional to him even when they harm him — Pym's worst behavior, Stark's contradictions, Cross's villainy, all registered with nuance). He does **not** project (he owns his failures, often excessively). He does **not** display psychotic denial of reality even under Pym Particle exposure or post-resurrection. The absence of these is a constitutional protective factor and should be noted in any future-risk assessment.

---

## 7.2 IMMATURE / NEUROTIC-ADJACENT DEFENSES

This is the bulk of the architecture. Lang lives here.

### 7.2.1 Rationalization (the master defense)

**Mechanism:** Post-hoc or pre-hoc construction of a morally acceptable reason for an action whose true motive is intolerable to the value system.

**Fingerprint:** *"I have to do this for Cassie."* This sentence, or its functional equivalent, appears at every major moral inflection point in the 45-year record. Original burglary of Pym: for Cassie (true, and rationalized). Power Broker work: for Cassie (partially true, mostly rationalized — by then he had alternatives he refused to model). Smaller breaches — lying to Avengers leadership about side activities, accepting payment from compromised sources, withholding from Cassie information about his employment — all routed through some variant of *protect her, provide for her, don't burden her.*

The defense is structurally elegant because **the love is real.** That is what makes it impregnable. He cannot be argued out of it because the truthful part of it is unfalsifiable. The defensive part — the conversion of *I want to take the expedient option* into *I must take the only option my daughter's welfare permits* — hides inside the truthful part like a parasite inside a healthy organ.

**Triggers:** Any decision where the expedient option violates an explicit value.

**Function:** Permits action under conditions his conscience would otherwise paralyze.

**Cost:** Strategic blindness. Once the rationalization engages, alternative-modeling shuts off. He has, in the record, repeatedly failed to even *consider* legitimate options that were available because the rationalization made the illegitimate option feel like the only one.

### 7.2.2 Minimization

**Mechanism:** Systematic downscaling of the magnitude of his own competence, his own transgressions, his own injuries, and the risks he is running.

**Fingerprint:** Verbal tics — "it's not a big deal," "I'm not really an Avenger, I just hang around with them," "nah, the suit does most of the work," "it was just a job that went sideways." Behavioral correlates — declining medical attention after serious combat injuries, downplaying the financial precarity that is actively driving his choices, describing federal felonies as "stupid mistakes."

**Triggers:** Bidirectional. He minimizes upward when his competence is praised (deflects credit) and minimizes downward when his failures are confronted (deflects gravity). Both directions serve the same goal: preserve the negative self-schema at its established calibration. Praise that lands too hard and criticism that lands too hard both threaten the schema's stability.

**Function:** Schema preservation. Affective regulation. Social lubrication — minimization reads as humility and makes him likable.

**Cost:** Prevents accurate self-assessment in either direction. He cannot price his own labor (small business failure in Miami), cannot calibrate the seriousness of his offenses (recidivism), cannot accept the genuine respect of his peers (lateral relationship deficits).

### 7.2.3 Humor / Self-Deprecation

**Mechanism:** Preemptive verbalization of the criticism the subject anticipates, in a tonal register that defuses it.

**Fingerprint:** Constant. The most reliable verbal signature in the record. Whenever a scene begins to load with the possibility of his being judged — by Cap, by Reed, by Cassie's mother, by Cassie herself in adolescence, by arresting officers, by reporters — the joke arrives within seconds. The jokes are not random; they are precisely targeted at the exact criticism he expects ("the ex-con joins the Fantastic Four," "world's worst dad reporting for duty," "great, now I owe Hank Pym another one"). He is naming the shameful frame before anyone else can.

**Triggers:** Any social moment of evaluative exposure. Mentor-facing situations especially. Cassie-facing situations chronically.

**Function:** Three layers. (a) Shame management — if he says it first, no one else's saying it can wound him. (b) Threat-reduction — a joking ex-con is non-threatening; a serious ex-con is suspicious. (c) Connection-bid — humor invites laughter, laughter is intimacy, intimacy is what he wants but does not believe he deserves directly.

**Cost:** Forecloses serious conversation. People who care about him — Cassie, repeatedly — eventually find the humor itself a wall. The defense that makes him approachable also keeps him unreachable.

### 7.2.4 Identification with the Aggressor — modified subtype: **Identification with the Grace-Giver**

**Mechanism:** Internalization of the values, mannerisms, and ethical posture of the most recent authority figure to extend him mercy.

**Fingerprint:** His "ethics" shift detectably across runs and across mentor-eras. Pym-era Lang is fastidious about the suit, deferential, technically precise — Pym's posture. Stark-era Lang carries Stark's bravado-with-an-apology-buried-in-it. The FF/Reed era introduces a more cosmic-curious, child-protective Lang. Cap-adjacent moments bring out an earnest dutifulness that is not natively his. This is not phoniness; it is genuine introjection. He becomes, in a slightly visible way, whoever last forgave him.

**Triggers:** Mercy. Specifically: a moment in which an authority figure declines to punish him for a transgression he expected to be punished for. The Pym scene in *Marvel Premiere* #48 is the founding instance and the template every subsequent grace-event re-runs.

**Function:** Provides an external ethical scaffold to a man who does not trust his own. Lets him operate morally by proxy.

**Cost:** Moral inconsistency across time. No durable internally-anchored ethics. Vulnerability to bad mentors (the Power Broker exploits exactly this — flattery + apparent trust = introject + compliance).

### 7.2.5 Reaction Formation (mild, episodic)

**Mechanism:** Conversion of an unacceptable impulse into its behavioral opposite.

**Fingerprint:** The compulsive, almost performative law-abidingness of his "clean" periods — over-correcting into rule-following in ways that read as anxious rather than principled. Returning library books on the day. Refusing minor traffic infractions. The Future Foundation period also has elements of this — he becomes a *protector of children* with an intensity that is partly grief sublimation (7.3.3) and partly reaction formation against the imagined version of himself who failed Cassie.

**Triggers:** Recent exit from a criminal episode. Post-incarceration adjustment windows.

**Function:** Identity-repair. Demonstrates to himself that he is not what he just was.

**Cost:** The over-correction is unstable; reaction-formation is metabolically expensive and reliably collapses under the next stressor, often into the original behavior.

### 7.2.6 Avoidance (relational, specific)

**Mechanism:** Behavioral and conversational steering away from material that would force confrontation with the negative self-schema.

**Fingerprint:** Topic-management with Cassie — specifically, the entire portfolio of "what dad does for money" conversations, deferred year after year until they detonate. Romantic avoidance — relationships terminated or never deepened at the moment they would require him to be known beyond the surface. Mentor-confession avoidance — he will tell a mentor he failed *after* he has been caught, never *before*, because telling before would require trusting that he will be forgiven *in advance*, and his template only accepts retroactive grace.

**Triggers:** Approach of intimacy past a specific depth threshold. The threshold is roughly: any conversation that would require him to assert, "I am a good man who did a bad thing," rather than, "I am a bad man you have been kind to."

**Function:** Schema preservation. Prevents the destabilization that would follow being known and accepted as he actually is, which is — and this is the paradox the entire defensive architecture exists to obscure — better than he believes.

**Cost:** The Cassie estrangement. Every failed lateral peer relationship. The thinness of his romantic record.

### 7.2.7 Intellectualization (limited, technical-domain only)

**Mechanism:** Conversion of emotionally loaded material into engineering/tactical analysis.

**Fingerprint:** Combat debriefs. Discussion of the Microverse. Discussion of Pym Particle physics. When the topic is technical, his affect smooths and his vocabulary precision spikes — observably a different register than his civilian speech. He retreats *into* the engineering when the surrounding context is emotionally loaded.

**Triggers:** Proximity to grief or shame, in a context where technical content is available as cover.

**Function:** Buys regulatory time. Permits participation in difficult conversations without affective flooding.
