**Cost:** Reinforces the perception (his and others') that he is "just the tech guy," underwriting the self-underestimation that costs him in non-technical domains.

### 7.2.8 Somatization (low-grade, inferable)

**Mechanism:** Conversion of psychological distress into bodily symptom.

**Fingerprint:** Inferential rather than directly observed. The record shows pattern of stress-bound minor injuries that read as carelessness — bumps, bruises, scrapes accumulated in periods of high psychic load that do not appear in periods of comparable physical activity but lower psychic load. Possible sleep disturbance (he is reliably awake at odd hours; whether this is post-incarceration sleep architecture or somatized anxiety cannot be cleanly distinguished). No documented chronic somatic complaints, but a man who lived through his daughter's cardiac childhood almost certainly carries a chest-region tension pattern that has never been clinically explored.

**Triggers:** Sustained low-grade stress without acute discharge channel.

**Function:** Pressure release.

**Cost:** Negligible at present levels; flagged for monitoring.

---

## 7.3 MATURE DEFENSES

These exist and are genuinely operative. They are what makes him functional, likeable, and — in his best moments — heroic.

### 7.3.1 Altruism (genuine, not pseudo-)

**Mechanism:** Pleasure and meaning derived from service to others, where the service is not primarily in the service of the self.

**Fingerprint:** The original burglary — committed at predictable cost to himself for his daughter's survival. The Future Foundation tenure — sustained care for children not his own. The pattern of physical risk-taking in combat that is *disproportionate* to mission requirements, where he places himself between threat and bystander with a reliability that exceeds tactical necessity. Crucially: he does not seek credit for any of this. The altruism is not performed for an audience.

**Discrimination from pseudo-altruism:** A pseudo-altruistic structure would require the gratitude or visibility of the recipient to sustain itself. Lang's altruistic acts are sustained in conditions where no recognition is forthcoming and often where the recipient never knows.

**Function:** Among his most stabilizing behaviors. The altruism is one of the few channels through which evidence of his own worth can occasionally penetrate the negative schema, because the schema cannot find a way to disqualify it.

**Cost:** Occasionally tips into self-sacrifice that is not strategically warranted — he will absorb a hit he could have evaded, take a charge he could have shared. Under the most extreme conditions this defense and the underlying schema can fuse into something that looks like willingness to die.

### 7.3.2 Sublimation

**Mechanism:** Channeling of unacceptable or unbearable impulses into socially constructive activity.

**Fingerprint:** The Future Foundation period is the textbook case — paternal grief, with nowhere to land after Cassie's death, channeled into custodianship of substitute children. But the pattern is broader. The Ant-Man identity itself is a sublimation: a man who broke the law to save his daughter, transmuted into a man who serves the law (loosely) to save other people's daughters. The size-shifting motif lends itself: he literally becomes *small* to do *large* things — a structural metaphor for the entire compensatory project.

**Triggers:** Bereavement, guilt, helplessness.

**Function:** High. This is one of the two defenses (with altruism) keeping the structure healthy enough to function across decades.

**Cost:** Sublimation is not the same as resolution. The underlying material remains live. When the sublimation channel is closed (no children to protect, no mission to run), the underlying material surfaces and routes back through the immature defenses.

### 7.3.3 Anticipation (selective)

**Mechanism:** Realistic forecasting of future affective challenges with pre-emptive psychological preparation.

**Fingerprint:** Selectively present. He anticipates well in *tactical* domains — pre-mission planning, threat-modeling on operations, contingency thinking in combat. He anticipates poorly in *personal* domains — the second-order consequences of his Power Broker engagement, the timeline on Cassie's loss of patience, the financial trajectory of his small business. The defense is real but compartmentalized.

**Function:** Where deployed, prevents avoidable crisis.

**Cost:** The compartmentalization is itself the deficit. The domains where he most needs anticipation are the domains where he least uses it.

### 7.3.4 Suppression (functional)

**Mechanism:** Conscious, deliberate setting-aside of distressing content to permit task focus, with intent to return.

**Fingerprint:** Combat performance. He visibly *sets down* whatever civilian crisis he is in to do the job, then picks it back up afterward. This is distinct from repression (unconscious) and dissociation (involuntary) — Lang's suppression is observably willed. He can also suppress grief when Cassie is present and needs the parent and not the wreck.

**Function:** Operational continuity. Parenting continuity.

**Cost:** The "return to it later" portion of the contract is unreliable. Material set aside frequently does not get picked back up, and migrates into the dissociative/somatic register.

### 7.3.5 Humor (mature subtype, distinct from 7.2.3)

**Mechanism:** Genuine perspective-giving levity that acknowledges difficulty without denying it.

**Fingerprint:** Distinguishable from the self-deprecating defensive humor by a different tonal signature — quieter, slower, often directed *outward* (offering perspective to a frightened civilian, a panicking teammate, a grieving colleague) rather than *at himself*. This is the humor he uses in genuine mentorship moments with Young Avengers and FF children. It does not deflect; it reframes.

**Function:** Among his most prosocial traits. Earns the loyalty of younger heroes who do not get this register from more imposing mentors.

**Cost:** None significant.

---

## 7.4 DEFENSE ARCHITECTURE — STRUCTURAL OBSERVATIONS

### 7.4.1 The Stack

Under stress, the defenses activate in a reliable sequence:

1. **Humor / self-deprecation** (immediate, automatic, social-surface).
2. **Minimization** (cognitive, within seconds).
3. **Intellectualization** (if technical content available).
4. **Suppression** (if a task is available to absorb attention).
5. **Avoidance** (relational steering begins, hours-to-days timescale).
6. **Rationalization** (engages once a decision is impending).
7. **Denial-in-action** (at the moment of transgression).
8. **Dissociative distancing** (post-event, for material too large to metabolize).
9. **Sublimation / altruism** (recovery phase, channeling the residue).

The stack is *consistent* across the 45-year record. A subject can be tracked through this sequence in real time during any major crisis arc.

### 7.4.2 The Load-Bearing Pair

**Rationalization + Identification-with-Grace-Giver** is the structural couplet that produces the recidivism. The rationalization permits the transgression; the introjected mentor-ethic then absorbs the post-hoc judgment and the cycle resets at the next forgiveness event. This couplet is the engine of the pattern noted in Section 1.

### 7.4.3 The Protective Pair

**Altruism + Sublimation** is the couplet that keeps the structure functional and the subject genuinely heroic. These two defenses do most of the work of converting the negative schema into prosocial output. Without them, the same personality would present as a melancholic recidivist with no heroic dimension. *With* them, he is a hero who keeps getting arrested.

### 7.4.4 The Missing Defenses

He does not use: **projection, splitting, idealization-devaluation cycling, omnipotence fantasy, primitive denial, acting-out in the borderline sense, passive aggression, hypochondriasis.** The absences pattern as *constitutional health* — the substrate is sound, the wounds are specific.

### 7.4.5 The Single Unbuilt Defense

He has never developed **acceptance of grace as deserved.** This is the missing structural element. Every defense in the catalogue operates downstream of the belief that he is in moral debt. A mature defense of *received-and-internalized worthiness* — the capacity to metabolize being forgiven as evidence of one's actual moral status rather than as a gift requiring repayment — would collapse the recidivism cycle by removing its fuel. Its absence is the through-line of the entire psychological file. Building it would constitute the only intervention that would change the prognosis.

— END SECTION 7 —


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# LONGITUDINAL PSYCHOLOGICAL PROFILE — SUBJECT: SCOTT EDWARD HARRIS LANG

## File Section 7 of 23 | Clinical-Developmental Trajectory, 1979–Present

---

## Prefatory Note on Methodology

This section reconstructs the subject's psychological evolution across approximately forty-five years of observable behavioral record (*Marvel Premiere* #47 through current Avengers-tenure appearances). Frameworks invoked: Bowlby/Ainsworth attachment theory; Vaillant's hierarchy of ego defenses; Beckian cognitive schema theory; Linehan's biosocial model of emotion regulation (for differential exclusion of BPD); Herman's complex trauma model; McAdams' narrative identity theory for self-concept work. Each decade is treated as a discrete clinical epoch with entry-state, dominant configuration, decompensations, adaptations, and exit-state. Where the subject's life-events are unusual to the point of breaking ordinary frames (death and resurrection, subatomic decompression, mentor-figure psychotic breaks at close range), the framework is named and its limits flagged.

The throughline: a personality structure that was probably constituted by age thirty as warm-conscientious-with-a-shame-core, and which has, in every subsequent decade, reorganized its defenses *around* that core rather than reworking it.

---

## EPOCH I — Pre-Suit Adulthood and Catalytic Crisis (late 1970s, *Marvel Premiere* #47–48 substrate)

**Entry-state.** The subject enters the observable record already mid-collapse. The pre-canon biography we can reconstruct from internal references — degreed electronics engineer, married to Margaret "Peggy" Rae, infant daughter, Stark International employment lost, downward economic spiral — implies a baseline personality that was *adaptive-conscientious* prior to crisis: a man whose self-concept was organized around competence, providership, and conventional masculine middle-class respectability. There is no antecedent record of impulse-control problems, substance use, or antisocial features. The first burglary is a *break*, not a culmination.

**Affect regulation.** At entry, affect is presumed normal-range but increasingly constrained by externalized financial shame. The subject's wife divorces him during or just after this period — diagnostic for the level of household stress and probably for emergent withdrawal, irritability, or affective flattening he is bringing home. He does not appear to have decompensated into rage or substance use; the regulation strategy is *constriction*, then *action*.

**Cognitive style.** Already the signature: engineering-analytical, narrowly tactical under pressure. The burglary is well-planned. He does not get caught by stupidity; he gets caught by the system functioning as designed. This is the first instance of what becomes the lifelong pattern — *tactical brilliance in narrow execution, catastrophic failure to model second-order consequence*. He plans the entry; he does not plan the life after the fence pays.

**Self-concept entry/exit.** He enters as "a man who provides." He exits — through arrest, conviction, incarceration, and Stark's vouch — as "a man who steals, who was caught, who was forgiven by a better man." That sentence is the load-bearing self-narrative for the next forty-five years. Everything subsequent is the elaboration of that one identity-statement.

**Catalytic event.** Cassie's cardiac diagnosis and the kidnapping of Dr. Sondheim. The second burglary (the Pym suit theft) is structurally identical to the first — competent crime in service of family — but moralized differently because the stakes are now a child's life. Pym's gift of the suit constitutes the **template trauma of grace**: the subject transgresses, expects punishment, receives instead an enlargement of trust. He does not metabolize this as deserved. He metabolizes it as *debt*.

---

## EPOCH II — The 1980s, Avengers-Adjacent Stabilization

**Dominant configuration.** Functional, sub-threshold-depressive, conspicuously *modest*. The subject takes the Stark electronics job, uses the suit sparingly, refuses to brand or expand the Ant-Man identity, declines repeated invitations to full Avengers membership in this era. This declination is psychologically overdetermined: it reads on the surface as humility, but the clinical reading is *self-handicapping* — staying small to remain within the moral territory he believes himself entitled to occupy.

**Affect regulation.** Markedly improved by the structure of legitimate employment, partial custody of Cassie, and the regularizing presence of mentor relationships (Pym at distance, Stark at workplace proximity, the Fantastic Four as occasional collaborators). Affect runs warm, slightly subdued, with a developing dry-humor register that is not yet the protective armor it later becomes — at this stage it is closer to genuine wit.

**Cognitive style.** Engineering work appears to be regulatory for him in itself. The cognitive narrowing observed under stress decompensates in stable periods into broad, curious, problem-solving engagement. He is a *better thinker* when not panicked, which is true of most people but is unusually pronounced in him because the panic-narrowing is so severe.

**Self-concept.** Stable but negatively valenced. He thinks of himself as the lucky ex-con, the man on probation from his own past. Evidence of competence (successful Stark work, successful heroics) is metabolized weakly — Beckian schema-maintenance: the data that would update the negative self-schema is filtered, attenuated, or attributed externally ("Tony trusts me," not "I am trustworthy"). Evidence of failure would be metabolized fully but does not arrive in this epoch, which is part of why the schema persists unchallenged — there is no decompensation to either confirm or finally refute it.

**Defenses (Vaillant hierarchy).** Predominantly mature-range in this period: sublimation (heroics as restitution), humor (developing), altruism (mentorship begins). Rationalization is dormant because no acute stressor activates it. Suppression is heavy — he does not talk about prison, does not talk about the divorce, does not talk about Cassie's medical fragility unless directly asked.

**Exit-state.** The decade closes with the subject in a deceptively healthy configuration. The negative schema is intact but quiescent. He has not been stress-tested in the specific configuration (financial collapse + Cassie threat + opportunity) that would reactivate the template. The clinical reading is that he is *not healed but unprovoked*.

---

## EPOCH III — The 1990s, Drift and the Reed Richards Cathexis

**Dominant configuration.** Low-amplitude drift. The subject moves in and out of the Fantastic Four orbit, takes on the role of Reed Richards' technical second during periods of Reed's absence. The mentor introjection shifts: where Pym had been the original grace-giver and Stark the workplace patron, Reed becomes the *intellectually idealized* authority, the man whose approval is metabolized as proof of one's own legitimacy.

**Affect regulation.** Largely intact, with mild dysthymic coloration. There is a thinning of his lateral peer relationships in this era — the Avengers cohort he came up alongside has changed personnel, and he does not appear to have invested in replacement peer bonds. The vertical bonds (up to mentors, down to Cassie) remain primary.

**Cognitive style.** Continues to develop technically. The Reed-collaboration period is one of the rare epochs where his intelligence is being externally calibrated by someone capable of seeing the actual ceiling rather than the modesty-performance. He responds to this with *more* modesty, which is diagnostic — being correctly assessed is more threatening to his self-schema than being underestimated.

**Self-concept.** Begins to admit a small additional clause: not just "the lucky ex-con" but "the lucky ex-con who is genuinely useful to Reed Richards." This is the first crack in the pure negative schema, but it is plastered over with attribution-to-the-mentor ("Reed thinks I'm useful") rather than internalized as self-knowledge.

**Romantic/intimate functioning.** Notably underdeveloped. Peggy Rae and other partners exist in the record but receive minimal investment relative to Cassie, mentors, and work. This is consistent with the formulation: the Cassie-cathexis has crowded out the lateral intimate slot. He is not avoidant in the classical sense — he is *occupied*.

---

## EPOCH IV — Early 2000s, Decompensation and Death

**Dominant configuration.** Increasingly stressed by ambient Avengers-grade combat exposure (an underacknowledged trauma load) and by Cassie's adolescence, which begins surfacing the conflict between the protective-fantasy father he wants to be and the actual ex-con father he is. He cannot quite manage either role and oscillates.

**Affect regulation.** Beginning to show subthreshold PTSD features: startle response, intrusive references to incarceration in inappropriate contexts (the joke-as-intrusion phenomenon), and a notable uptick in conflict-avoidance behaviors with Cassie. He does not yet meet criteria for any specific Axis I presentation, but the regulatory margin is narrowing.

**Cognitive style.** Tactical-narrow under sustained moderate stress. He is making more expedient decisions, smaller ones, more often. None individually rise to the level of his original transgressions, but the *frequency* of micro-rationalizations is climbing.

**Catastrophic event.** *Avengers Disassembled* (2004). Killed by Scarlet Witch's reality-breakdown, atomized, no warning, no preparation, no narrative arc — exactly the kind of death that is psychologically corrosive even for the survivors. For the subject himself, the death is consciousness-terminating; there is no experience of it. But the *resurrection* will have to integrate it retroactively, which is a clinical problem with no real-world analogue and only weak frame-fit.

**Self-concept at death.** Unchanged. He dies still believing he is the man who was forgiven, still paying interest on the Pym debt.

---

## EPOCH V — Posthumous Interregnum and Resurrection (2004–2010)

This epoch is necessarily inferential. The subject is non-existent in the observable record; Cassie processes her father's death by becoming Stature in the Young Avengers, which is itself a sublimation — she takes his identity-technology and his cause and routes her grief through them. When the subject is restored by Wiccan's reality-warping in *Avengers: The Children's Crusade*, he reenters a world he has not lived in, into a daughter he has not raised through her hero-emergence, into a Young Avengers cohort that knew him only as legend.

**Re-entry affective state.** Initially euphoric (reunion with Cassie) — and then, within the same arc, catastrophic. Cassie is killed by Doom. The subject loses, in the space of weeks of subjective time, the entire reason he died.

**Clinical formulation of the resurrection-into-bereavement sequence.** There is no clean framework for this. The closest analogues are (a) returning combat veterans whose primary attachment died during deployment, and (b) survivors of a near-death experience followed immediately by the loss of a child. Both populations show extremely high rates of complicated grief, treatment-resistant depression, and dissociative features. The subject shows all three to varying degrees but is *not floridly symptomatic*, which is itself worth flagging. He appears to dissociatively distance from his own death (the flippant references begin here and never stop) and to channel the Cassie-loss into the substitute-paternal Future Foundation work rather than into a fully expressed grief presentation.

This is high-functioning but not healed. The grief is encysted, not metabolized.

---

## EPOCH VI — The Future Foundation Period (Hickman through Fraction/Allred, ~2010–2013)

**Dominant configuration.** Textbook sublimation in service of unbearable affect. He leads the FF children's team — a literal substitute-paternal role — and is observably better at it than his prior self-concept would have predicted. He is patient, structurally available, slightly distant in the way that a grieving father with other people's children is forced to be in order not to either over-attach or recoil.

**Affect regulation.** The structural role contains him. There is a phenomenon in bereavement clinical work where high-functioning grievers regulate by *taking on caretaking obligations to others*, and the obligations themselves provide the scaffolding that absent internal regulation would otherwise need to supply. The subject is in this configuration for most of this epoch.

**Cognitive style.** Surprisingly expansive. Around the FF kids he thinks broader and longer-range than at any other point in the record. The hypothesis: when the immediate stressor is not his own daughter but other people's children, the cognitive narrowing reflex does not engage, and his actual intelligence — which the file should record as substantially above the surface presentation — is visible.

**Self-concept.** A small revision: he is now "the man who was forgiven, who failed his daughter, who is trying to be useful to other people's children." The new clause is no less negative than the old, but it is *operational* — it gives him something to do every day that is consistent with the schema. This is not growth, it is stable accommodation. The schema has incorporated the new loss without restructuring.

**Defenses.** Sublimation dominant. Humor present but blacker than in the 1980s. Suppression still heavy — he does not speak of Cassie unless asked, and even when asked, deflects. Identification with the aggressor begins to invert into identification with the *mentor*: he is now occupying the role Pym, Stark, and Reed occupied for him, and is the grace-extender to the FF kids, but he does not seem to register this structural symmetry. If he registered it, it would force the recognition that grace can be extended by people who are themselves not done, not whole, not "better men" — which would in turn force the recognition that *his* grace from Pym was also given by a flawed man, and was therefore neither magical nor unearned. He does not make this connection. The schema protects against it.

---

## EPOCH VII — Miami / Spencer Period (2015–2017)

**Dominant configuration.** The full template reactivates under specifically the conditions that originally installed it: financial precarity, threat to Cassie (now estranged adolescent/young adult requiring ongoing relational and material investment), opportunity (Power Broker's offer). The subject relocates, opens Ant-Man Security Solutions, fails at the small business — and the small-business failure is clinically interesting in itself: he is competent enough to run the business but cannot bear to charge clients adequately, cannot bear to refuse pro bono work, cannot tolerate the perceived greed of legitimate commerce. The negative schema is interfering with the very legitimacy he is ostensibly trying to build.

**Affect regulation.** Visibly degraded. Humor escalates into protective armor — the self-deprecation is no longer wit, it is preemptive shame-management deployed prophylactically in nearly every interaction. The wry register that was charm in the 1980s is now a tell.

**Cognitive style.** Catastrophic narrowing under Power Broker engagement. He performs the rationalization ("for Cassie, just this once, I can manage it") in front of the reader with near-conscious awareness that it is a rationalization, which is the most clinically advanced state the subject ever reaches — *seeing the defense as it operates and using it anyway*. This is not denial; this is volitional self-deception, which is harder to treat than denial because the patient is participating.

**Self-concept under stress test.** The schema *wins*. Given the opportunity to act consistent with a revised self-concept (legitimate businessman, recovered ex-con), he sabotages it and reverts. The reversion confirms the negative schema, which is the schema's covert purpose — it is structured to be self-validating.

**Cassie rupture.** The relational consequence is the loss of Cassie's trust over precisely the pattern she has been watching her whole life. The clinical significance is that the *one* attachment that has organized his entire personality breaks under the weight of the very behavior the attachment supposedly justified. The rationalization eats the thing it was protecting. He does not appear to fully integrate this paradox; if he did, it would be a structural break in the schema.

**Exit-state.** Incarcerated again. The carceral re-exposure compounds the original carceral trauma — there is a known phenomenon of accelerated psychiatric deterioration on second incarcerations relative to first, and the subject's flatness and constricted affect during and after this sentence are consistent with this.

---

## EPOCH VIII — Recent Stabilization (Ewing *Ant-Man* 2022, Avengers tenure, present)

**Dominant configuration.** Performed self-awareness as a stabilization strategy. The subject now *jokes about being the screw-up* with such fluency that the joke functions as a complete defensive structure: by claiming the identity preemptively, he denies anyone the chance to assign it to him, which superficially looks like integration but is more accurately *fortification of the schema*. He has not revised the self-concept; he has made it socially manageable.

**Affect regulation.** Returned to functional baseline. Combat performance excellent — and the file should register that he is, as previously noted, paradoxically healthier in acute crisis than in ordinary life, because crisis discharges the chronic pressure his ordinary defenses must continuously manage.

**Cognitive style.** Increasingly broad in low-stress conditions; still narrows reliably under Cassie-stressors, though Cassie's increased autonomy (she is functionally an adult hero in her own right) has reduced the frequency of activations. The pattern is unbroken; it is simply less often triggered.

**Self-concept.** Substantively unchanged from 1979. The negative core schema ("I am the man who steals, who fails, who needs to be forgiven") remains load-bearing. What has changed is its *packaging*: the schema is now wrapped in forty-five years of accumulated humor, accumulated mentor-grace-events, and accumulated heroic record. The packaging is thick. The core is identical.

---

## SYNTHESIS — Trajectory Across the Whole

Plot the eight epochs against time and three things become visible.

**First**, the affect-regulation curve is roughly stable across the lifespan with two notable dips (2004 pre-death period; 2015–17 Miami collapse) and one notable elevation (FF Future Foundation period). The subject is, by adult-functioning standards, a well-regulated person whose regulatory failures are stressor-specific, not characterological. This rules in adjustment-spectrum and rules out personality-disorder spectrum.

**Second**, the cognitive-style curve shows clear bimodality across the entire life: broad-curious-creative under stable conditions, narrow-tactical-rationalizing under specifically the financial-plus-Cassie stressor configuration. The bimodality is *motivated*, not constitutional. He is capable of the broader cognition; he is unable to access it when the specific template is active. This is the most clinically tractable feature of his presentation and the one most amenable to intervention if intervention were ever offered.

**Third**, the self-concept curve is essentially *flat*. Across forty-five years, despite resurrection, despite paternal loss, despite multiple incarcerations, despite genuine heroic achievement at Avengers grade, the core self-schema has not revised. New clauses are added; the core sentence does not change. This is the most striking longitudinal finding in the file. Most subjects with comparable life-events show schema revision in at least one direction (either decompensation into worse self-evaluation or growth into better). Lang shows neither. The schema is *protected* — actively, by the entire defense structure — because revising it would require him to confront the central unmetabolized fact of his life: that Pym's grace in 1979 was not magical and not unearned, that he has been paying interest on a debt that was never owed, and that he is, and has always been, a man whose actual conduct over forty-five years has more than substantiated the trust that was originally extended.

He cannot let himself know this. Knowing it would dissolve the schema, and the schema is the structure around which the entire personality has organized. The pattern is durable not because it serves him but because it *is* him, as he currently exists.

— END SECTION 7 —


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL

## Subject: LANG, Scott Edward Harris
## Section 4 of 11 | Cross-reference: §3 (Psychological), §2 (Medical), §6 (Behavioral Patterns)

---

## 4.1 Framing Note on Methodology

The subject has never, on the available record, sat for a formal psychiatric evaluation. Court-ordered pre-sentencing reports exist from both incarcerations (NY State, mid-1979; federal Miami, post-2016) and are summarized below where their contents can be reconstructed from behavioral residue. The remainder of this assessment is built from forty-five years of observed behavior, longitudinal pattern-matching, and inference from documented stressor-response cycles. Diagnostic categories below are offered in the DSM-5-TR / ICD-11 vernacular for compatibility with downstream files; the underlying clinical reality is, as always, dimensional rather than categorical.

A standing caution: the subject's exposure to Pym Particles and to Microverse-scale subatomic transit is biologically uncharacterized. Any neuropsychiatric assessment of this subject is conducted in the knowledge that an unknown chronic neurological insult may be present and may eventually express. The absence of overt psychotic-spectrum sequelae (cf. Pym, H., documented dissociative-identity and psychotic-spectrum presentations) is a present finding, not a permanent one.

---

## 4.2 Principal Formulation

The most defensible primary formulation is **Recurrent Adjustment Disorder with Mixed Disturbance of Emotions and Conduct (F43.25 analog), superimposed on Prolonged Grief Disorder (F43.81 analog) and chronic Post-Traumatic Stress Disorder, partial-threshold (F43.10 analog), against a substrate of Persistent Depressive Disorder, mild, with early onset (F34.1 analog).**

The structure of that formulation matters more than any single label. The subject is not, primarily, a man with a disorder. He is a man whose baseline (mildly depressive, conscientious, warm, intelligent) is repeatedly destabilized by a specific stressor configuration, and whose decompensation expresses itself behaviorally (conduct) rather than affectively (mood) or perceptually (psychosis). The grief and trauma layers are real but second-order; they shape the *form* of decompensation. The adjustment-disorder layer is the *engine*.

### 4.2.1 Why Adjustment Disorder, Recurrent, Is Load-Bearing

Across the 1979–present record, the subject's clinically significant maladaptive behaviors cluster, without exception, around an identifiable stressor onset and remit within months of stressor resolution. The original 1979 burglary cycle: precipitant (job loss → daughter's medical crisis) → six-week behavioral disorganization → discrete criminal act → arrest → remission of symptoms within carceral structure. The mid-2010s Miami cycle: precipitant (business failure + Cassie's renewed medical and social precarity) → escalating compromise with Power Broker over approximately eighteen months → arrest → remission. The interstitial periods — and there are decades of them — show no antisocial conduct, no persistent dysphoria of clinical severity, no occupational impairment beyond that attributable to felony record. This is the textbook longitudinal signature of recurrent adjustment disorder rather than a personality-level pathology.

The "mixed disturbance of emotions and conduct" specifier is required because each episode contains both a dysphoric component (covert; the subject conceals it under humor) and a conduct component (overt; the criminality or rule-breaking that gets him noticed).

### 4.2.2 Why Prolonged Grief Disorder Is Present and Unresolved

The death of his daughter in *Children's Crusade* (Doom, 2012) constitutes an exposure that meets the gateway criterion for what DSM-5-TR added in 2022 as Prolonged Grief Disorder. The narrative reversal of that death does not extinguish the lived experience or the somatic memory. Observable residua, persistent across the post-2012 record:

- **Identity disruption around fatherhood:** the subject continues to behave as a man who has failed his daughter terminally, even when Cassie is alive and standing next to him. The grief schema outlasted the loss.
- **Avoidance of grief-adjacent stimuli:** notable reluctance to revisit the events of *Disassembled* and *Children's Crusade* in conversation, deflected with humor each time.
- **Emotional numbness selectively around Cassie's adulthood:** the subject struggles to register her competence as Stature/Stinger; his internal representation of her remains pre-adolescent.
- **Substitutive caretaking:** the Future Foundation period (Fraction/Allred *FF*, 2012) is a sublimated grief response, not a free vocational choice.

This is, in clinical language, a partially resolved complicated bereavement that the narrative universe "fixed" without the subject ever being permitted the grief work.

### 4.2.3 Why Chronic PTSD, Partial-Threshold

Criterion A exposures are stacked: kidnap-recovery operations from the original Sondheim rescue, Avengers-scale combat across four decades, two incarcerations, his daughter's death, his own death and atomization. Criterion B (intrusion): present at low intensity — occasional intrusive references to his own death, surfaced as flippancy, which is a recognized PTSD presentation in male subjects with high pre-trauma humor baseline. Criterion C (avoidance): present, narrowly — the subject avoids substantive conversation about Cassie's death and about the prison years. Criterion D (negative alterations in cognition and mood): the negative self-schema documented in §3 is partially attributable here, though it predates the major traumas and cannot be wholly assigned to them. Criterion E (arousal and reactivity): hypervigilance toward law enforcement, mild startle, sleep architecture probably disrupted (no polysomnography available; collateral suggests early-morning waking, fragmentary dreams).

The case for *partial-threshold* rather than full-threshold PTSD rests on functional preservation: the subject sustains relationships, executes complex work, and does not show the social-occupational collapse that full PTSD typically produces. The trauma signature is present, embedded, and chronic, but it does not run the personality. It modifies the personality at the margins.

### 4.2.4 Why Persistent Depressive Disorder, Mild, Early Onset

The negative self-schema is not adequately accounted for by adjustment, grief, or trauma alone — it predates all three. The subject's pre-1979 self-narrative (reconstructible from his own references) already contains the architecture of inadequacy: a man who got the Stark job and felt he hadn't deserved it, who lost it and felt he had. Persistent low-grade negative self-evaluation, chronic mild pessimism specifically about his own trajectory (never about others'), humor that performs the depressive function of preempting injury — these are dysthymic features, mild, lifelong, ego-syntonic enough that the subject does not perceive them as illness. He perceives them as accurate.

No major depressive episode is documented. Hedonic capacity is preserved; energy is preserved; concentration is preserved; suicidal ideation is not present in the record (a point of clinical relief, given the cumulative load).

---

## 4.3 Symptom Presentation in Observable Behavior

The translation from diagnostic language to surveillance-relevant behavioral markers is as follows.

**Stressor-onset markers (early; 2–6 weeks pre-decompensation):**
- Increase in self-deprecating humor frequency, measurable in conversation transcripts; jokes shift from situational to self-referential.
- Sleep onset latency increases; subject reports being "fine" while collateral observers note pre-dawn ambulation.
- Phone-call frequency to Cassie increases but call duration decreases — checking-in behavior rather than connection behavior.
- Subject begins declining social invitations from peer heroes, accepting from peripheral or morally ambiguous contacts.
- Financial-records review (where available) shows the characteristic pattern of small consolidation moves followed by a single large precipitating shortfall.

**Mid-episode markers (4–12 weeks pre-arrest or pre-incident):**
- Information management with Cassie — selective omission rather than outright lying, which is the subject's tell. He cannot sustain direct lies to her and does not try; he reroutes conversations.
- Increased contact with tertiary network: ex-cons from his original sentence, technical contractors from the Miami security business, the periphery of the Power Broker network.
- Rationalization vocabulary surfaces in recorded speech: "just this once," "I have a plan," "Cassie doesn't need to know," "I can handle it."
- Suit usage pattern changes: prior to compromised periods, the subject begins using Pym Particles for tasks that are sub-heroic — surveillance, lock bypass, evidence retrieval. This is a reliable early indicator.

**Acute decompensation markers:**
- A discrete criminal act, almost always *technically clean* (a function of his engineering competence) but *strategically catastrophic* (a function of the cognitive narrowing).
- Post-act flatness; the subject does not show elation or relief, he shows a brief affect-vacancy that collaterals have described as "going quiet."
- Compliance with arrest when caught — no flight, no resistance. The carceral structure is, perversely, a regulatory relief.

**Remission markers:**
- Within structured custody, the subject's affect, sleep, and humor regulate within 10–14 days. This is diagnostic. Personality-disordered subjects do not remit on this timeline; situationally stressed subjects do.
- Re-engagement with mentor figures; the subject writes letters (Pym, Stark, Rogers, Richards have all received them) framed as accountability, functionally as petitions for re-extension of grace.

---

## 4.4 Course Over Time

**1979–1989 (Establishment phase):** Single major episode (the originating burglary) followed by a decade of sub-clinical stability. The subject's protective factors — Stark's vouching, the structuring effect of Avengers-adjacent work, Cassie's young-childhood vitality — held the dysthymic baseline below clinical threshold.

**1990s–early 2000s (Plateau phase):** Functional stability. Custody arrangements with Peggy Rae are amicable but emotionally restricted; the subject's reduced romantic investment frees affective bandwidth for Cassie and for hero-work. Sub-clinical throughout.

**2004 (Death event):** Atomization in *Disassembled.* No psychiatric assessment possible during the deceased interval. Note that the experience of being killed by a reality-warping event is unprecedented in any clinical framework.

**2010–2012 (Resurrection and re-loss):** The most severe psychiatric period in the record, though it does not present as such because the subject's defenses mobilize fully. Re-entry into a world where his daughter has aged into adulthood and then is killed in front of him constitutes a sequential double-trauma without precedent in conventional clinical literature. The Future Foundation sublimation is the saving response.

**2015–2017 (Miami decline):** Full recurrent adjustment episode, the most behaviorally florid in the record. The Spencer-run documentation is, for our purposes, a clinical case study. Decompensation arc complete; remission via re-incarceration.

**2020s (Stabilization phase):** Emergence of meta-awareness. The subject now jokes about being the screw-up, which is a partial integration but a partial integration only — it metabolizes the shame without addressing the underlying schema. This is what therapists call *insight without change.* Prognosis: stable until the next stressor configuration recurs.

---

## 4.5 Comorbidity

- **Adjustment Disorder × Prolonged Grief:** the grief makes each recurrence of adjustment disorder more severe, because the Cassie-threat dimension of the precipitant configuration carries additional charge.
- **PTSD × Persistent Depressive Disorder:** the trauma reinforces and validates the pre-existing negative self-schema. Each trauma is metabolized into evidence for the dysthymic worldview ("of course this happened to me").
- **Carceral re-adaptation syndrome × adjustment disorder:** two incarcerations have produced a paradoxical relationship to custody — it is feared in anticipation and regulating in experience. This complicates risk assessment, because the subject does not behaviorally avoid arrest with the urgency that a non-carcerally-adapted subject would.
- **No substance use comorbidity.** Notable and protective. The dysregulation discharges through action and not ingestion.

---

## 4.6 Differential — What the Subject Is Not

The behavioral surface of this subject (recurrent criminality, charm, susceptibility to bad influence, mentor-orientation, parenting failures) invites several mis-formulations. Each must be ruled out explicitly.

### 4.6.1 Not Antisocial Personality Disorder

The most common misreading on paper. Two felony arrests, a documented willingness to deceive, repeated rule-breaking — a careless reader of the record sees Cluster B and stops. Wrong.

Antisocial PD requires (i) pervasive disregard for the rights of others, (ii) lack of remorse, (iii) deceitfulness as a stable trait, (iv) conduct disorder before age 15. The subject fails every one of these. (i) His criminal acts are precisely calibrated to minimize harm to others; the original burglary returned the suit; the Miami arc victimized institutional and corporate targets, not individuals. (ii) Remorse is excessive, not absent — the entire negative self-schema is constructed of remorse. (iii) Deceit is stressor-bound and shame-laden; baseline relational style is unusually candid. (iv) No pre-15 conduct disorder; the historical record (Stark hiring background check, reconstructed) shows a conventional educational trajectory.

The Hare PCL-R, if administered, would score in the low single digits. This is not the man.

### 4.6.2 Not Narcissistic Personality Disorder

The hero identity could invite this differential. It does not survive scrutiny. Narcissistic PD requires grandiosity, need for admiration, lack of empathy, exploitation. The subject's self-concept is *too negative* for grandiosity; his need is for forgiveness, not admiration (a distinction with profound prognostic implications — forgiveness can be metabolized, admiration cannot); empathy is intact and frequently the destabilizing factor; he is exploited rather than exploiting.

The hero name (Ant-Man — small, undignified, deliberately deflationary) is, on its own, near-diagnostic of the *absence* of narcissistic structure. A narcissist does not choose Ant-Man.

### 4.6.3 Not Borderline Personality Disorder

Surface features (relational intensity around Cassie, fear of abandonment, identity uncertainty) suggest the question. The differential fails on structural grounds. Borderline requires identity diffusion; the subject's identity is the opposite — *over-stable* around a fixed negative schema that he protects from contradicting evidence. Borderline requires generalized abandonment panic; the subject's abandonment fear is specific to Cassie and absent in other relationships. Borderline requires affective instability with rapid mood shifts; the subject's affect is unusually regulated, with decompensation expressed in behavior rather than mood. No self-harm history. No splitting in object representation.

### 4.6.4 Not Attention-Deficit/Hyperactivity Disorder

The "scattered," self-deprecating surface presentation can read as ADHD. It is not. The subject's attentional difficulties are stressor-bound and motivationally specific, not pervasive across domains. His engineering competence requires and demonstrates sustained focus of a kind ADHD does not permit. His tactical performance in acute crisis is the opposite of an ADHD presentation. The scatter is *performed* and *defensive*, lowering perceived threat for an ex-con seeking re-acceptance. Diagnostically: nil.

### 4.6.5 Not a Substance Use Disorder

Notable for its absence given the load. The subject discharges through action; the action is the agent of relief that would otherwise be sought in substance. This is protective until the discharge action is itself the pathology (cf. recurrent criminality), at which point the absence of substance use is a hollow protective factor.

### 4.6.6 Not a Bipolar Spectrum Disorder

No documented hypomanic episodes. The acute-crisis high-function state could superficially suggest hypomania; it does not. Hypomania does not remit cleanly when the crisis ends. The subject's crisis-function does, returning to dysthymic baseline within hours.

### 4.6.7 Not Pym-Particle-Induced Psychiatric Syndrome (provisional)

The clearest available comparator subject (Pym, H.) presents with a documented neuropsychiatric profile attributed in part to Particle exposure: dissociative features, psychotic-spectrum breaks, mood instability. The subject Lang shows none of these. Two possible explanations: differential cumulative dose (Lang uses the technology far less aggressively and at less extreme size variance than Pym), or differential constitutional vulnerability. Either way, the present finding is that Particle-induced psychiatric syndrome is NOT contributing to the current presentation. This finding requires periodic re-evaluation.

### 4.6.8 Not Malingering, Not Factitious

The subject does not perform symptoms for secondary gain. If anything, he under-reports — the documented humor-based deflection is *anti-performance* of distress. Where he has been offered support (Avengers medical, Stark resources) he has typically declined or minimized. The dysphoria is real and concealed.

---

## 4.7 Etiological Synthesis

The subject is best understood as a constitutionally warm, mildly dysthymic, conscientious, technically gifted adult whose formative crisis (job loss → criminal solution → incarceration → unearned-feeling reinstatement) installed a permanent associative template equating *love-for-Cassie* with *justified transgression* and *survival* with *being-vouched-for-by-a-better-man.* Each subsequent major stressor (Cassie's medical crises, Cassie's death, financial collapse, threat to the second-generation surrogate children) reactivates the template with high fidelity. The diagnostic surface (adjustment, grief, trauma, dysthymia) is downstream of this single etiological structure.

The clinically critical inference is this: the subject's pathology is not what he has done. It is what he believes about why he was forgiven for doing it. The original act of grace from Pym in 1979 was extended in response to observed behavior — that is, it was *earned*, in any reasonable sense. The subject has spent forty-five years experiencing it as *gifted*, and structuring his entire adult psychology around servicing an imaginary debt. Every recurrent episode is, in part, an unconscious attempt to re-enact the original transgression-and-rescue in order to re-experience the rescue — because the rescue is the only configuration in which he feels accurately seen.

This is the intervention point. No intervention has ever been offered, and the subject has never sought one. He is unlikely to.

---

## 4.8 Risk Assessment

- **Risk to self:** Low. No suicidal ideation in the record. Reckless self-endangerment in crisis contexts is real but discriminable from suicidality (it is purposive, other-directed, and protective).
- **Risk to others (direct):** Very low. Empathy intact; violence consistently other-protective rather than instrumental.
- **Risk to others (indirect, via competence misapplied):** Moderate to high during decompensation episodes. The subject's technical and tactical abilities, in the service of a compromised judgment, have produced and could again produce significant downstream harm.
- **Risk of recurrence:** High, conditional on stressor configuration. The pattern has held for forty-five years across four major chroniclers; absent intervention, expect another episode within the next stressor cycle that combines financial precarity with threat-to-Cassie (or threat-to-substitute-child).
- **Risk of catastrophic decompensation:** Low under current conditions. Would escalate sharply in the event of (a) final estrangement from Cassie, (b) Cassie's death (recurrence), or (c) a betrayal by a mentor-figure he has structurally elevated.

---

*— END SECTION 4 —*
*Continue to §5: Personality Architecture.*


## Behavioral Atlas

# BEHAVIORAL ATLAS: SCOTT EDWARD HARRIS LANG

## File Subsection 5-B / Longitudinal Micro-Behavioral Mapping
### Source base: 45 years observed conduct, four primary writer-eras, cross-referenced against in-universe surveillance footage, SHIELD/Avengers debriefs, NYSDOCCS and Florida DOC custodial records, and Cassie Lang's own corroborating testimony where extant.

---

## I. BASELINE / CALM STATE

When unobserved threat is absent and no Cassie-related variable is active, Lang's resting presentation is *deceptively low-key*. The casual observer reads him as a slightly tired man in his forties of unremarkable build, unremarkable affect, and faintly self-amused expression. This reading is wrong in one specific direction: the alertness is fully online, it is simply masked.

**Postural baseline.** Sits slightly forward of the seat-back, never quite committed to the chair — a carceral residue (chairs in custody are not safe to lean into; you keep your weight where you can rise from it). When standing, weight rests on the rear leg, lead leg slightly turned out, hands either in pockets or one hand at the back of the neck. The neck-rub is the single most reliable Lang tell across all eras: it appears at the onset of social mild-discomfort, at the moment of being complimented, and at the instant of beginning a sentence that contains a lie of omission. Frequency increases monotonically with the magnitude of the omission.

**Eye behavior.** Comfortable eye contact in low-stakes settings, but a documented pattern of *breaking left and down* before answering questions about his own history. Scans rooms on entry — door, exits, weight-bearing furniture, sightlines — within roughly four seconds of arrival, then visibly relaxes the scan. Does not maintain hard surveillance after the initial sweep. The sweep itself is half engineering reflex (he is mapping load paths and electrical runs as much as threats) and half carceral.

**Speech tempo at baseline.** Mid-register, slightly nasal New York vowels surviving even after years in Miami/San Francisco. Tempo is moderate, with a habit of trailing off the back end of declarative sentences when he is uncertain whether the listener is interested. Recovers the sentence with a small upward intonation ("…anyway") when he decides they aren't. Frequent use of self-interrupting clauses — "I mean, that's not — what I'm saying is —" — which sound like distractibility but on tape are revealed to be active syntactic management: he is editing the sentence in real time to avoid claiming more competence than he believes he has the right to claim.

**Manual fidgets.** Constantly working something small with his hands — a coin, a bolt, a torn napkin corner, the band of a wristwatch. Not pathological, not anxious — this is engineer-hand: the same neurology that lets him strip and reassemble the suit's regulator manifold in low light cannot tolerate idle digits. Distinct from his stress-fidget (see III).

**Eating.** Fast, slightly furtive, finishes plate before companions are halfway through. Custodial conditioning. He is unaware of this and would deny it if asked.

**Sleep architecture (calm periods).** Reportedly five-and-a-half to six hours, falls asleep quickly, wakes between 3:40 and 4:20 a.m. with reliability sufficient that he no longer sets an alarm. The pre-dawn wake-window is when he reads technical material, answers email he has avoided, and stares at the ceiling. He calls this "his good hour," and resents anyone who interrupts it.

**Domestic baseline.** Apartments and houses across his published life share three constants: tools out, dishes done late, and at least one photograph of Cassie in a sightline from wherever he habitually sits. The photo is never current. He preferentially keeps images from ages where the relationship was easier — generally pre-adolescence Cassie, generally a moment he is in the frame.

---

## II. LOW-GRADE STRESS / SOCIAL DISCOMFORT

This is the band where the humor turret rotates online. Stress in the mild range — a meeting going long, a mentor being mildly disappointed, a journalist asking a personal question — produces a measurable uptick in *self-deprecating output per minute*. The jokes are good. They are also defensive. The diagnostic feature is that the humor preempts criticism rather than responding to it: he names his own failing before the room can.

**Verbal tells:**
- Frequency of the construction "*I know, I know* —" rises sharply. He uses this to acknowledge a deficiency before it is raised, which prevents the interlocutor from raising it.
- Increased use of the third-person self-reference ("typical Lang," "this is a Scott Lang move"). This is dissociative-lite: he is putting a small narrative distance between his ego and the behavior under discussion.
- Apologizes for things that have not occurred yet ("sorry if this is dumb, but —"). Pre-apology rate is a reliable index of social pressure.

**Physical tells:**
- Neck-rub (above) escalates from once-per-five-minutes baseline to once-per-minute or higher.
- Adjusts cuffs of long-sleeved garments — a learned tic from prison transition periods where he kept his hands occupied to avoid them being read as a threat. Persists civilianly.
- Smile flickers on without reaching the eyes; the genuine smile (which crinkles the outer orbicularis) is reserved for Cassie, for genuinely funny things said by other people, and — diagnostically — for the moment a mentor laughs at one of his jokes.

**Decision behavior.** At this level he is still operating his full conscience. He will defer, he will hedge, he will not lie outright. He will, however, begin *managing information* — choosing what not to mention, framing decisions already made as decisions still under consideration to avoid argument. The management is small and venial at this band.

---

## III. ELEVATED STRESS / PRESSURE STATES

Operationally defined: financial precarity, mentor disapproval that lands, the realization that he has been seen doing something he wished unseen, or the early-warning stages of a Cassie-threat.

**Postural shift.** Loses the forward lean; sits *back*, arms either crossed at the sternum or hands flat on thighs. This is the carceral defensive posture — minimize surface, present nothing grabbable. Pulse-visible-at-temple if observation is close enough.

**Verbal shift.**
- Sentences shorten.
- The humor *thins out*; jokes become noticeably less funny because they are now load-bearing rather than ornamental. He keeps cracking them because stopping would be a confession.
- Begins what surveillance analysts have labeled the *"Lang loop"* — a three-clause structure: (a) acknowledge the problem, (b) name a half-solution, (c) deflect from the full solution. ("Yeah, that's bad. I'll, uh — I'll handle the morning thing, and we'll figure the rest out.") The third clause never resolves. The loop is how he buys time without committing.
- Begins to drop his daughter's name into unrelated sentences. This is a tell of impending rationalization-engine startup. When Cassie enters the rhetoric, the frame for an upcoming transgression is being built.

**Physical fidgets, stress variant.**
- The engineer-hand object (coin, bolt) is *gripped* rather than rolled. Knuckles whiten.
- Right thumb works the joint of the left thumb in a small, repetitive press. Self-soothing, dating to the original 1979 burglary preparation per his own offhand admission in a *Marvel Premiere* flashback panel.
- Increased throat-clearing. He drinks more water than he wants to.
- Foot bounces under tables, almost always the left foot, ball of foot only, low amplitude, high frequency.

**Sleep degradation.** The 3:40–4:20 wake window shifts earlier, to 2:30–3:00, and is no longer a "good hour" — it is rumination. He will reach for his phone, look at Cassie's last message, not reply, and put the phone down. He will do this multiple times per pre-dawn.

**Eating shift.** Loses the appetite first, then loses interest in the *idea* of meals. Subsists on coffee and whatever single carbohydrate is closest to the workbench. Drops three to five pounds across a sustained pressure period; this is visible in the jawline by week two.

**Decision behavior at this band.** This is the band in which his cognitive narrowing engages and where he stops modeling second-order consequences. The narrowing has a specific signature: he will be able to describe, with full clarity, *the next move* in tactical detail, and will be unable or unwilling to describe *the move after the next one.* If asked "and then what?" he will answer in generalities and pivot. The pivot is the diagnostic.

---

## IV. ACUTE THREAT / COMBAT

Paradoxical inversion. Where chronic stress degrades him, acute threat *organizes* him. This is the most striking single feature of his behavioral record and is consistent across every writer who has handled him in action.

**The transformation, in observed sequence:**
1. *Onset (first 0.4–0.8 seconds).* Stillness. Not the freeze of fear; the stillness of an engineer who has just been handed a problem and is determining the gradient. Eyes go to threat, then to room geometry, then to threat again.
2. *Commitment (within ~1.5 seconds).* Begins moving — and he is *not* a hesitator in combat. The same man who cannot decide whether to text his daughter back will commit to a plan involving subatomic shrinkage and a thirty-story drop in the space of a breath.
3. *Operational mode.* Talkative. Lang in combat *narrates* — to himself, to ants, to enemies, to teammates on comms, to no one in particular. The narration is partly tactical (he is thinking out loud, which is faster for him than thinking silently), partly affect-regulating (it keeps him calibrated to a wry register that prevents fear escalation), and partly social (it makes his teammates trust him faster than his résumé would).
4. *Use of size-shift.* Reliable behavioral pattern: he *shrinks before he punches.* Other size-shifting heroes (Pym in his Giant-Man eras, Cassie as Stature) reflexively go large under threat. Lang reflexively goes small. This is diagnostic — Lang's threat-response is to *disappear from the threat-frame and reattack from an unexpected vector*, not to overpower. It is a thief's instinct surviving inside a superhero's tactics.

**Combat tells:**
- Telegraphs nothing facially before action. The face stays in its baseline wry set.
- Will throw the first joke approximately ten seconds into any sustained engagement. The first joke is calibration — gauging the room.
- Defaults to *protecting the smallest person on the field*, regardless of tactical priority. This has been operationally inconvenient on at least three documented occasions.
- Self-sacrificial range is wide. Will accept disproportionate personal risk without visible deliberation when a non-combatant is in frame. The deliberation has been pre-completed by the negative self-schema (see Section 3 of main file): he has rated his own survival as low-value capital, and he spends it accordingly.
- After action: hands tremble for between four and eleven minutes. He keeps them in his pockets or on a piece of equipment until they stop. He does not want anyone to see.

---

## V. INTIMACY / VULNERABILITY

The category in which he is *least* skilled and most visibly so.

**With romantic partners.**
- Affectionate, present, attentive on the surface. Beneath: notably difficult to access at depth.
- Does not initiate conversations about the future. Will participate if pressed; will not lead.
- Treats his own emotional content as an imposition. Will downgrade the severity of his bad days when asked. "I'm fine" is delivered with sufficient warmth to read as authentic and is, across canon, almost never accurate.
- Sex: physically warm, emotionally guarded, leaves the bed first in the morning to "make coffee," which is also a way to be facing a stove rather than a face when the partner wakes.
- Has never, in published canon, told a romantic partner the full carceral story unprompted. They have always learned from third parties.

**With Cassie.**
- This is the *only* relationship in which his defenses partially come down, and even here they reconstitute fast.
- Voice modulates softer, vowels slow, the tempo-trailing disappears entirely. Sentences finish.
- Physical proximity behavior: stands closer to her than to anyone else, but does not initiate contact — waits for her to. The hug-protocol is always Cassie-initiated. He returns hugs with full-bodied force and is reliably the last to release.
- Conversational avoidance pattern: anything in his life that would disappoint her gets reframed into a smaller, funnier version of itself. She has caught him in this approximately as often as he has done it. The catch is what eventually broke the relationship in the Spencer arc.
- When she is in the room he checks for her every 90–120 seconds in his peripheral vision. Unconscious. Has done this since she was four. Will do this when she is forty.

**With mentor figures (Pym, Stark, Rogers, Richards).**
- Body language miniaturizes — shoulders narrow inward, head tips slightly down on first interaction of any meeting.
- Speech volume drops 10–20%.
- Defers reflexively to their judgments even when he has better data. Will then quietly act on his better data anyway, framing it post hoc as their idea.
- Cannot accept praise. Praise from these figures is metabolized via deflection: "well, the suit did most of it" / "you would have done the same" / "yeah, lucky break." The deflection is automatic and arrives within two seconds of the praise.
- Will not ask them for help even when help is the obviously correct move. Asking would be drawing on the credit line he believes he has already overdrawn.

**With peers / lateral relationships.**
- Slow to form. Will spend years in mutual proximity to a colleague before risking actual peer-bond behaviors (advice-giving, criticism, vulnerability disclosure).
- Once formed, durable. Lang does not casually discard peer bonds. The FF kids, the surviving Young Avengers, the small handful of crime-adjacent contacts he has kept honest with — none of these get dropped.
- With other ex-cons: visibly more relaxed. Speech tempo quickens, profanity rises, the carceral postural caution drops. He does not need to perform reformedness around people who already know the inside of a cell.

---

## VI. GRIEF

The grief register has been observed at sustained length only twice in canon: the FF run (post-Cassie's death by Doom) and the immediate aftermath of his estrangement from her in the Spencer arc. The two presentations are different and the difference is informative.

**Acute bereavement (post-Cassie's death, Children's Crusade / early FF):**
- *No public collapse.* No weeping in front of others, no extended absences from duty. Anyone reading from the outside would assess him as "holding up well." This assessment is wrong.
- *Function preserved by overfunction.* Took on the FF leadership role almost immediately. The substitute-children sublimation engaged within weeks. Work hours doubled. Sleep halved.
- *Physical contraction.* Weight loss, color in the face going grey, the wry smile flattening out to a polite smile that does not crinkle the eyes for nearly a year of in-canon time.
- *Verbal tell.* Stopped saying her name aloud in casual reference. The avoidance was so consistent that it itself was conspicuous. He could discuss her in operational contexts (the Doom revenge frame) but could not say "Cassie said once that —" in a memory-anecdote register without his voice failing mid-clause. He stopped trying.
- *Object behavior.* Began carrying a small object of hers — a charm, a hair tie, varies — in his left front pocket. Touches it when transitioning between activities.

**Estrangement-grief (post-Spencer break):**
- Different register. Where death-grief produced overfunction, estrangement-grief produced *slippage* — return to expedient illegality, the Power Broker arc, the small-business failures.
- Because estrangement contains a moral wound (she chose to leave; he gave her reason), this grief reactivates the negative self-schema directly, and the schema's behavioral output is *transgression that confirms the schema.* He becomes more the man she said he was, which is grief's worst expression in his repertoire.
- Drinking up-ticks marginally — not pathological, but observable. Two drinks where one would have been baseline.
- Sleep further degrades; the 3:00 wake becomes a 1:30 wake, and he stops trying to use the hour productively. Stares at phones, walls, ceilings.

**Universal grief tells (both registers):**
- Eats standing up.
- Stops repairing things around the apartment that he would normally fix immediately. The broken thing sits.
- Begins long projects he will not finish — the half-stripped engine, the unsoldered board, the unwritten letter.
- Re-watches or re-reads content from a period in his life he is mourning. Old footage. Old photos. The re-engagement is private and dense.

---

## VII. VICTORY

Lang does not know how to win.

**Immediate post-victory behavior:**
- *Deflects the credit instantly.* The deflection is automatic and arrives before anyone has offered him credit, which sometimes confuses witnesses ("I wasn't going to — okay").
- *Asks about other people first.* "Is everybody okay" / "did we get the civilians out" / "where's [smallest team member]" is the reliable opening sequence post-engagement, before anyone has had time to ask about him.
- *Quiet for a beat longer than expected.* Other heroes celebrate; Lang takes thirty to ninety seconds of quiet first. He is, on the record, running an after-action audit — what almost went wrong, what could have gone wrong, what he failed to model. The audit always finds something. Then he rejoins the celebration with a joke.
- *Physically backs out of the spotlight.* Press photo behavior, repeatedly documented: ends up at the edge of frame. Not by accident. When pulled into the middle, posture shrinks half an inch.

**Sustained post-victory periods (rare):**
- Discomfort rises rather than falls. Stable positive periods make him itchy because they expose the gap between his self-concept and the evidence. He will, with reliability sufficient to predict, find a problem to solve, a person to help, a job to take — *something* to do that puts him back in the posture of repaying rather than receiving.
- The Pym-grace template is reactivated in unexpected directions during good periods: he becomes more likely to extend grace himself to younger heroes who have screwed up, often beyond what is warranted. He is paying it forward without realizing the original debt was always imaginary.

---

## VIII. DEFEAT

Tactical defeats he metabolizes well. Moral defeats he does not.

**Tactical defeat (mission failed, plan didn't work, suit malfunctioned mid-fight):**
- Immediate diagnostic mode. What broke, why, fix protocol. Lang in failure-diagnosis is one of the most focused versions of him observable in the record.
- No blame-displacement. Will name his own error first and accurately. This is one of the few self-evaluations he performs honestly, because engineering failure is morally neutral to him in a way that personal failure is not.
- Will work without sleep until the failure is understood. Eighteen-to-thirty-six-hour bench sessions are documented.

**Moral defeat (was caught lying to Cassie, was caught in a crime, let down a mentor):**
- *Full schema confirmation* — and visible. Color goes out of the face. Voice goes flat. The wry mask falls.
- Apologizes too fast and too much, which paradoxically reduces the apology's credibility. The over-apology is itself a defense — if he flattens hard enough, the other party will sometimes back off, and he treats their backing-off as the closest he can come to being forgiven.
- *Will not advocate for himself.* Even when factually unjustly accused, he will accept disproportionate blame, because the negative self-schema treats unjust accusation as merely *miscalibrated true accusation* — he was probably guilty of something close enough.
- Behavioral residue lasts months. The next several decisions will be made under the gravitational pull of the moral defeat, often producing the next moral defeat. The cycle is the canon's single most persistent narrative engine for the character.

---

## IX. UNDER OBSERVATION / SURVEILLANCE-AWARE BEHAVIOR

Lang assumes ambient surveillance more than most subjects of his cohort. This is partly carceral, partly Avengers-operational, partly genuine technical literacy — he knows what is and isn't easy to capture.

**Counter-surveillance tells:**
- Will tap a phone twice on a table edge before laying it screen-down. Unconscious habit. Functions as nothing technically; functions as ritual.
- Speaks in oblique reference when discussing anything operationally sensitive in any space he does not own. Will not name people; uses positional descriptors ("our friend uptown") or first initials.
- Sweeps any new room for cameras and microphones within the first two minutes. The sweep is not theatrical; he does it while doing something else — picking up an object, pacing the room as if restless, leaning against a wall whose interior he is feeling for wiring.
- Sits with line-of-sight to entries. Never with his back to the door. Will rearrange seating to achieve this and pretend the rearrangement is about the light.
- Cash preference for any transaction he wishes uncorrelated. Knows what cards leak and what cards don't.
- Burner cycle: maintains at least two non-primary phones at all times in unstable periods, rotates them on irregular intervals. The irregularity is genuine — he does not want his rotation to itself be a pattern.

**When he knows he is being watched:**
- Performs *more* normally. The "off-camera" Lang is fractionally tenser than the "on-camera" Lang, which is the inverse of most subjects. Carceral conditioning: under direct observation he relaxes into the role of the unthreatening, because he has practiced it.

---

## X. RITUALS, ROUTES, AND MICRO-HABITS

The dense granular layer.

- **Coffee.** Black, two cups, the first while standing at whatever counter is nearest, the second sitting down. Will drink other people's bad coffee without complaint and will quietly improve the apparatus the next time he visits.
- **Pre-mission ritual.** Before suiting up: checks the regulator manifold by hand (he does not trust the diagnostic readout), runs his thumb along the edge of the helmet seal, exhales once, taps the chest plate twice with the heel of his palm. The taps date to the original Pym suit in 1979 and have never been omitted in the published record.
- **Post-mission ritual.** Removes the helmet first, gloves second, breathes for a count of approximately six before speaking to anyone. Anyone who interrupts the six-count gets a slightly delayed and slightly distant first response. He does not realize he does this.
- **Phone-and-Cassie ritual.** Opens her last message thread once on waking, once before sleep. Does not always reply. Sometimes drafts replies he does not send. The drafts accumulate in unsent form across years; this has been depicted directly.
- **Walking routes.** Varies them when in any phase of his life that includes criminal exposure. Repeats them comfort


## Daily Life, Routines & Rituals

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 7: DAILY LIFE, ROUTINES & RITUALS

## Subject: Scott Edward Harris Lang
## Surveillance Frame: Composite week, post-Miami stabilization era, generalizable across most non-crisis periods of adult civilian record.

---

## 7.1 The Architecture of a Day

The subject's day is built on a foundational misalignment: he keeps the sleep schedule of a man who has worked night shifts (legal and otherwise) for most of his adult life, but he tries to perform the morning rituals of a custodial father. The two schedules war with each other and neither wins.

**Sleep onset** typically falls between 01:20 and 02:40. He does not get into bed at any consistent hour. He falls asleep where he stops moving — couch, desk chair, occasionally the floor next to whatever electronics project he was disassembling. When he does make it to a bed, he sleeps on his side, facing the door. Carceral residue: he has not slept facing a wall since his first sentence. He keeps a phone face-down within arm's reach, ringer on, never silenced — Cassie could call.

**Sleep duration** is 4.5 to 6 hours on a normal night, with one or two "crash" nights per fortnight where he goes down at 21:00 and sleeps eleven hours, surfacing groggy and apologetic to no one. He does not use an alarm. He wakes to ambient light or to the specific frequency of a text-message buzz, which he registers in deep sleep where a generic notification will not rouse him. This is trained, not natural.

**Wake** is between 06:40 and 08:15. The first ninety seconds of consciousness are spent confirming his location — eyes open, ceiling check, window check, *what city, what bed, what year*. Resurrection-derealization residue, low-grade and chronic. By second 100 he is reaching for the phone to confirm no missed call from his daughter or her mother.

## 7.2 The Morning Stack

He does not eat breakfast in the kitchen. He eats breakfast standing up, in the doorway between kitchen and whatever serves as a living room, leaned on the jamb. This is consistent across at least three documented addresses. Surveillance hypothesis: it is the only sightline in any of his apartments that covers both entrances simultaneously. He has never articulated this and would deny it if asked. Breakfast itself is unserious — coffee (drip, never espresso, made too strong because he eyeballs the grounds and consistently overshoots), a piece of toast eaten dry or with peanut butter applied with the back of a spoon because he has misplaced every butter knife he has ever owned, and on better days a banana. He keeps bananas. He always has bananas. They are the one grocery he reliably replaces.

The coffee mug rotation is diagnostic. He has approximately fourteen mugs, of which he uses three. The three are: a chipped Stark Industries 1980s-vintage employee mug (sentimental, used on good mornings); a child's mug with a unicorn on it that Cassie picked out when she was seven (used on hard mornings, never washed properly, ring stains accumulating like tree rings); and a generic diner mug stolen from a coffee shop he visited twice in Miami (used on neutral mornings, no emotional weight, his "default"). Which mug he reaches for in the first ninety seconds is a more reliable mood indicator than anything he will say aloud that day.

He showers in the morning only about half the time. The other half, he showers at night, sometimes both. Showers are short, hot, and end abruptly — he does not linger. He talks to himself in the shower at audible volume. Surveillance microphones would capture rehearsals of conversations he is dreading: text to Cassie, request for a loan extension, explanation to a Foundation colleague about why a prototype is late. He rehearses the other person's lines too, in a softer voice. He does not know he does this.

He dresses out of a chair, not a closet. Clothes accumulate on a single chair near the bed; clean clothes go into the chair from the laundry, dirty clothes go into a basket near the chair, and the chair is the system. He owns approximately eleven shirts in active rotation, predominantly henleys, soft button-downs worn open over t-shirts, and one or two thermal long-sleeves regardless of climate (Miami included — the thermals are talismans, not garments). Jeans are dark, mid-weight, replaced only when destroyed. Footwear is sneakers, low-top, broken in past structural integrity; he replaces them with the identical model when forced. He owns one pair of dress shoes and resents them.

## 7.3 Pockets — Itemized

A search of his person on any given day, surveillance-confirmed, will yield:

- Phone (mid-tier, two generations behind current, screen cracked in upper-right corner — has been since at least the *Astonishing* run and he refuses to repair it; the crack is a fidget surface for his right thumb).
- Wallet, leather, bifold, contents in disarray: license, two debit cards (one of which is reliably overdrawn), library card (Miami-Dade), three to five receipts he intended to log for taxes and will not, a single folded photograph of Cassie at approximately age six (creased, soft as cloth, replaced perhaps once a decade).
- Keys on a carabiner, not a ring. Carabiner clips to belt loop when working, lives in pocket otherwise. Five to seven keys, three of which he could not identify.
- A small multitool, Leatherman-class, gifted by a mentor figure years ago. He has lost it twice and recovered it both times. It is the single object whose loss would unsettle him disproportionately.
- A pen, usually black, usually borrowed and never returned.
- Loose change he never spends; he is a coin-accumulator who empties pockets into bowls and jars and forgets the jars exist.
- An Ant-Man containment unit — a single canister, suit and helmet compressed at minimum size — clipped inside the waistband or in an interior jacket pocket, depending on garment. He carries it *always*. Even to dinner with Cassie. Especially to dinner with Cassie. He has not been unarmed in this sense since 1979.

## 7.4 Work Hours, Such As They Are

Lang does not have a job in the salaried sense for most of the surveillance record.
